Current Commentary

The Crisis in Suiyuan 48

— Yi

The biggest obstacle in Sino-Japanese relations is undoubtedly all the "established facts" created by the Japanese military in North China. Now, the diplomatic authorities of the two countries are racking their brains to adjust their relations. The Japanese military seems to be intensifying the creation of new facts of aggression, deepening the rift between the two countries. This is something we cannot help but regret. According to Suiyuan telegrams, the Japanese military recently instigated the Chahar bandit Wang Ying's troops to invade Xinghe in eastern Suiyuan. Although this intrusion did not succeed due to the brave defense of Fu Zuoyi's troops, it shows that Japan is determined to occupy Suiyuan in the short term to complete the final stage of its plan to annex Inner Mongolia.

Japan's ambition to annex Inner Mongolia has long been manifested in the division of Xing'an into four provinces. Since then, Japan has been monopolizing the feudal princes of Inner Mongolia and buying off bandits and traitors, trying to separate the provinces of Chahar and Suiyuan from our country. Last year, Prince De, under Japanese coercion and exploitation, declared independence in Biximiao. The puppet army of Li Shouxin occupied six counties in northern Chahar and established a military government in Zhangbei, changing the county system to a league system. Thus, most of Inner Mongolia's territory has actually fallen. Now, even the surviving Suiyuan and southern Chahar are under the serious threat of Japan's military deployment.

However, even today, we cannot despair of the future of Inner Mongolia. We must know that the people of Inner Mongolia not only cannot be separated from the Chinese nation under international law, but also, due to their own awareness, they will also try their best to resist the oppression of aggressive forces. This can be proven by many past facts. Japan coerced Prince De to summon the various leagues and banners, which in turn led to the dissolution of the Mongolian Political Affairs Committee and the rebellion of the Bailingmiao Training Corps. This is one. Four senior officials of the Xing'an puppet government, including Ling Sheng, were executed by the Japanese because the local Mongols opposed conscription and confiscation of pastures. This incident made the Mongols of various leagues and banners deeply feel the falsehood of Japan's "good neighborliness" propaganda. The establishment of the Suiyuan Mongolian Leagues and Banners Political Affairs Committee is said to have been prompted by this. This is two. This year, the puppet army of Li Shouxin, armed with modern weapons supplied by Japan, repeatedly invaded Taolin but was repelled by the Suiyuan Mongolian army. This is three.

The anti-Japanese sentiment of the Mongols has clearly caused many twists and turns in Japan's annexation policy. Japan's work to seize Suiyuan is therefore planned very skillfully and carefully. The recent guerrilla-style intrusions by small bandit troops are preparations for a large-scale invasion in the future. The activities of the Japanese army on the Ping-Sui Railway are arrangements to isolate the Suiyuan defense forces. And the military conference held by Prince De in Jiabusi earlier this month also has serious implications.

Today's situation increasingly confirms that Japan, in order to complete its annexation policy, is determined to acquire Suiyuan. Japan's goal in annexing Mongolia is, on the one hand, to surround Outer Mongolia to threaten the Soviet Union, and on the other hand, to lay the foundation for North China, and then extend its reach to the Central Plains of our country. Therefore, the survival of Suiyuan is of great importance to world peace and the future of China. For the sake of world peace and inviolable territorial sovereignty, we must do everything we can to preserve the endangered Suiyuan. We firmly believe that as long as the people of the whole country have a common determination, the ruined Inner Mongolia can still be saved.

The Tripartite Currency Agreement of England, America, and France Takes Effect: The Establishment of a So-Called New Gold Standard Controls Exchange Rates and Eliminates Speculation 49

(Washington) Secretary of the Treasury Morgenthau declared today that the tripartite currency agreement is a new type of gold standard. Its main effect is to transfer the power to buy and sell gold from irresponsible speculators to the government. From the American point of view, the purpose of the agreement is to protect commerce from the impact of drastic exchange rate fluctuations without affecting the value of the dollar. The agreement took effect today. From now on, the sale of gold will be managed by the Federal Reserve Bank of New York as the agent of the U.S. government, at a price of $35 per net ounce, plus a handling fee of 0.025%. (Reuters, 13th)

(London) The Ministry of Finance announced today that the technical cooperation arrangements agreed upon by the British and American financial authorities have been completed. As a result, the U.S. Secretary of the Treasury will issue new regulations allowing any country that provides reciprocal convenience to purchase gold in the United States to exchange for U.S. dollars. The British government has allowed the U.S. authorities to enjoy this convenience in London. This daily operational approach will be of great benefit to the technical movement and control of exchange rates. Similar arrangements have now been agreed upon with the Bank of France, enabling effective cooperation between the three centers of London, Washington, and Paris. Reuters has learned that this approach is purely reciprocal and aims to facilitate technical movements without changing policies. The pound sterling remains a free currency and is not affected in any way. If there are surplus funds in New York due to exchange control intervention, they will be converted into gold at a fixed price. The same will be done when there are surplus funds in London and Paris, depending on the daily situation and at mutually agreed prices. (Reuters, 13th)

(Washington) Secretary of the Treasury Morgenthau announced today that the United Kingdom, France, and the United States will adopt a "new gold standard" starting on Tuesday, allowing mutual exchange of cash for banknotes. This measure can be cancelled at any time within 24 hours. The difference from the previous gold standard is that the new measure only allows governments to move cash and does not allow speculative profiteering. The Secretary also said, "We now welcome other countries to participate." The new measure also stipulates that the names of countries that can engage in cash transactions will be announced daily. Currently, the Federal Reserve sells cash at a price of US$35 per ounce, plus a handling fee of 0.025%. After the implementation of this new plan, foreign banknotes can be exchanged for cash, private speculation can be avoided, and exchange rates can be stabilized. The Secretary also said, "This is the second step in the government's implementation of world monetary policy, which has not been effective domestically," but its impact only affects the price of the dollar abroad and not domestically. If its implementation hinders the recovery of the United States, the United States can cancel it. (National Telegram, 12th)

Implementation of the New Gold Standard System 50

The Basis for International Currency Stability

(New York) Commerce Newspaper editor Paul Boden declared today that the "new gold standard" of the United Kingdom, France, and the United States is convincing enough to make people believe that the world's leading countries are indeed planning to revive world trade by stabilizing currencies and reducing commercial barriers. There have been many questions recently about the value of the tripartite currency agreement. Now we have the government's answer. This agreement may become the basis for currency stability around the world in the future. Although it may not have significant immediate effects, its benefits will be seen over time, just as after the stabilization of the German mark in 1924, world commerce flourished until it was interrupted in 1929. The new tripartite agreement may also have the same effect. (National Telegram, 12th)

Ample Cash Reserves in the United States 51

The Ban on Gold Exports is Virtually Lifted

Denver, Colorado - President Roosevelt declared in a speech here today that the gold and silver reserves of the United States are sufficient to recover all currency with a surplus, so the monetary system of the United States is the most stable in the world. (Reuters, 12th)

(New York) Regarding the mutual freedom of the United Kingdom, France, and the United States to purchase gold, financial experts on Wall Street have recently commented that the United States originally prohibited the transport of gold to the United Kingdom and France. Now that the exchange equalization funds of the United Kingdom, the United States, and France can purchase gold from each other to prevent huge fluctuations in the exchange market, the above ban has been virtually lifted. When the authorities of these countries established the currency agreement, they must have already discussed it, but they waited for the financial legislation of the countries concerned to be harmonized with this new approach before announcing it today. (Havas, 12th)

(London) British officials are unwilling to comment on the "new gold standard" agreed upon by the United Kingdom, France, and the United States. Chancellor of the Exchequer Chamberlain only said that "the pound sterling is already free" and solemnly declared that the agreement is "purely technical and does not change policy." Local newspapers today all carried similar arguments, and between the lines, it can be seen that the United States has completely or partially lifted the ban on cash exports. (National Telegram, 12th)

Views of the Japanese Financial Authorities 52

There is No Need to Devalue the Japanese Yen Again

(Tokyo) Regarding the establishment of a free gold movement agreement between the exchange equalization funds of the United Kingdom, the United States, and France, the Ministry of Finance authorities observed as follows: the tripartite exchange stabilization agreement that occurred as a result of the devaluation of the French franc is expected to be followed by some kind of stabilization work. The Secretary of the Treasury's statement can be regarded as the first step in realizing this work. The result is to stabilize the exchange rates between the three countries without transporting cash. Only by transferring the amount to the counterparty country can the fluctuation of exchange rates be prevented. In the past, the United States allowed gold to be transported to gold standard France. The result of this time recognizing it for the United Kingdom as well is that the exchange rates between the three countries can temporarily find a stable point. Also, when the tripartite agreement was established, Japan was asked for understanding and hoped for support. Japan has expressed its approval, because there is no intention to depreciate the value of the Japanese yen again. Therefore, the rumor that Japan refused to support the tripartite agreement is a complete misunderstanding. (Domei News Agency, 13th)

The World Catholic Eucharistic Congress Will Be Held in the Philippines Next Spring 53

Manila - The 33rd World Catholic Eucharistic Congress will be held here from February 3rd to 7th next year. 300,000 to 400,000 people will attend the meeting, and the world will be able to listen to part of the ceremony by radio. According to Catholic leaders preparing for the Congress, an estimated 5,000 to 10,000 Catholics from all over the world will gather in Manila by sea and air. At least 300,000 of the Philippines' 11.5 million Catholics will also attend the meeting. Radio broadcasting has already been tested today. At that time, Pope Pius XI's blessing will also be broadcast by radio from the Vatican to the Congress venue. In the United States, the entire country will be rebroadcast by radio networks. The local church board has asked the authorities to use 1,000 young Filipino Catholics to assist the police in maintaining traffic. The venue is located in the Luneta Grand Park on the edge of Manila Bay, and extremely large electric lights will be installed on freight trucks, which will be brightly lit every night. A large altar 35 meters high will be built on the bay side facing the park, and thousands of seats will be specially built in the park. Construction will begin in a few weeks. (National Telegram, 12th)

Successful Arctic Flight, Journey of More Than 20,000 Kilometers 54

Moscow Correspondence - Soviet hero Vasily Molokov has arrived in Moscow, completing his great flight, passing through all the important locations in the Soviet Arctic region. Under extremely difficult climatic conditions, Molokov flew over 26,000 kilometers, from Krasnoyarsk via Ayan (Okhotsk Sea Port), Petropavlovsk (in Kamchatka), Commander Islands, Bering Strait, Wrangel Island, Cape Schmidt, Tiksi Bay, Cape North, Dickson Island, Vaigach Island, Arkhangelsk to Moscow. Thus, Molokov has for the first time completed a miracle of flying the entire Great Northern Air Route, proving that regular east-west exchanges can soon be carried out along the entire Arctic coast.

The aircraft Molokov was on was: USSRN2, a twin-engine all-metal flying boat, motor "M17" type, equipped with the latest aviation instruments, with a lifeboat, a rubber boat for five people, and a complete set of utensils for the crew.

In addition to Molokov and his assistant pilot Bobby and Mov, co-pilot Mishchenko, navigator Ritzren, the plane also carried the Deputy Director of the Northern Sea Route Administration, Bugarvinov, two officials from the shipping line, and a special reporter from the Truth Daily. The plane also carried food, gifts and books for the wintering expedition teams, all of which prove that air cargo transportation can be established in the Arctic Ocean. (TASS, September 19th)

British Cabinet to be Reorganized 56

(London) A partial reorganization of the British Cabinet may take place in the near future, and is currently being discussed by politicians. The reason for the cabinet reshuffle is that the Secretary of State for Scotland, Collins, is recuperating in a Zurich hospital in Switzerland due to illness and cannot return to his post for a while. A replacement must be found. However, Collins belongs to the National Liberal Party. The National Cabinet is organized jointly by the Conservative Party, the National Liberal Party, the National Labour Party. Now, if Collins leaves his post, the original distribution of cabinet seats among the three parties will lose its balance. Some politicians are now planning a remedy, that is, to promote the Minister of Transport, Sir Ballysher, to the rank of cabinet member, either to continue to serve as Minister of Transport, or to change his position to Secretary of State for Scotland. After all, it is not easy to find another National Liberal Party member to take on the post of Secretary of State for Scotland, and Sir Ballysher was originally a member of the National Liberal Party. Therefore, some people advocate grafting to maintain the original balance of the various parties in the cabinet. (Havas, 12th)

U.S. Republican Presidential Candidate Criticizes the New Deal; Roosevelt Responds 58

Cleveland, USA - Republican presidential candidate Landon gave a speech here today, vigorously attacking the waste of the New Deal, saying that the current government, in times of serious depression, still has the energy to edit guide books and analyze geological fossils. Although Landon did not criticize the New Deal's disaster relief funds, he claimed that the government used the funds to create a huge political organization to preserve its regime and to make one-sixth of the nation's population live in another economic world, controlled by a hopeless federal bureaucracy. In fact, the solution to the disaster relief problem lies entirely in recovery, and the way to recovery lies in the government stopping controlling people's lives. If I am elected, the Republican Party will first collect the facts of the unemployment problem, and then the local authorities will handle the disaster relief, with the federal government only providing economic assistance. (National Telegram, 12th)

Denver, USA - Republican presidential candidate Landon severely criticized President Roosevelt's New Deal, accusing him of wasting national funds. Today, President Roosevelt gave a campaign speech here, responding, saying that when he took office, the nation's economic activity was completely stagnant, and he had to take strong action. "The government allocated funds to enable unemployed workers to obtain work, and provided loans to people in various industries. It is true, but the government's actions were based on the opinions provided by technicians and specialized institutions in various regions of the country, especially in the agricultural and mining centers, not reckless. Later, the industries were revived thanks to the government's efforts." President Roosevelt then said that the government now has sufficient gold reserves to redeem all circulating banknotes. "The stability of our country's currency system is unparalleled in the world." Finally, the President reiterated the declaration he made ten days ago in Pittsburgh, saying that the government will save expenses and increase revenue, and the budget can be balanced and the national debt can be reduced in one or two years. (Havas, 12th)

Denver - President Roosevelt gave a speech to the crowd here today, emphasizing the progress of the U.S. economy, believing that the government budget can be balanced in one or two years, and saying that if elected for the job again, he will continue agricultural policies and relief plans. The President's speech did not mention Republican presidential candidate Landon, but this was a response to Landon's speech in Chicago, saying that Republican leaders called our great plan a waste, which is ridiculous, because their states and local governments had financial panic and first asked the federal government for relief. The term "consistency between words and actions" cannot be found in the Republican campaign dictionary. (National Telegram, 12th)

The German Government Notifies Britain of Opposition to the Anglo-Russian Naval Agreement, Believing that Britain Has Made Excessive Concessions to Russia; The Prelude to Revising the Anglo-German Agreement; The Anglo-American-French Treaty is Also Shaken 59

(London) The German Chargé d'Affaires in Britain, Bismarck, submitted a note to the British Foreign Office today, expressing opposition to the Anglo-Russian naval treaty draft because it deviates from the principles of the 1936 Anglo-French-American naval treaty, believing that the British side has made excessive concessions to Russia in the Anglo-Russian draft treaty. The most important of these is the provision that if Japan violates the qualitative restrictions of the tripartite naval treaty, the Soviet Union can also use it as an example. Although the German note did not mention revising the Anglo-German naval treaty, foreign naval circles fear that Germany's move may be a sign that if Britain's concessions to Russia are not changed, Germany will also propose a revision request. Since the Anglo-Russian naval restriction treaty cannot be signed without Germany's approval, the Soviet Union has stated that Germany should also accept any qualitative restrictions. If Germany and Russia cannot compromise on qualitative restrictions, then Britain's efforts to promote the principles of the tripartite naval treaty to the Baltic Sea and Scandinavian countries will be in vain. Even the tripartite naval treaty itself will lose its effectiveness due to the escalator clause. The only hope is that all parties can reach a satisfactory solution. (Reuters, 12th)

(London) The German government today delivered a new note to Britain, stating that if the Anglo-Russian naval agreement is signed, the German government will have to consider expanding its navy. The German government believes that the Anglo-Russian agreement will overturn the naval balance of power in Europe, especially will disrupt the balance of power in the Baltic Sea, so it requires a revision of the Anglo-German naval treaty signed in London in June 1935 to remedy this. (National Telegram, 11th)

America's Attitude Towards Pacific Fortification is Believed to be Achievable Tacit Understanding Key Lies in Japan 60

(Washington) Most observers here believe that Britain's proposal to maintain the status quo of Pacific fortifications may promote a general naval disarmament understanding between Britain, the United States, and Japan. Some semi-official circles here initially opposed the British proposal because it would make the United States give up the cheapest and safest way to deal with Japan's expansion of its navy, but it was learned today that the United States may consider this proposal if Japan can reliably guarantee not to expand its navy. According to non-official sources, if Japan is willing to announce its three-year, five-year, or ten-year naval construction plan in advance, the United Kingdom, the United States, and Japan may be able to reach a tacit understanding on fleet strength. This tacit understanding will be a gentleman's agreement between the three countries on naval and Pacific defenses, without mentioning a ratio system, so as to avoid Japan's dislike and achieve the effect of avoiding naval competition. The mutually beneficial points in the London and Washington treaties should be retained. (National Telegram, 12th)

Therefore, Germany has asked Britain to reconsider the Anglo-Russian agreement, and when the Anglo-Russian agreement is concluded, it will also demand that the Anglo-German agreement be made public, which must be said to be a matter of course. The German side was especially dissatisfied with a cartoon displayed at the Communist Party rally, which was used to symbolize the German leader, Adolf Hitler. Responsible officials in France stated that this matter falls within the jurisdiction of the publishing law, which stipulates that foreign leaders must not be insulted. The German Embassy can file a lawsuit against the organizers of the Communist Party rally on this basis. However, it is reported that Forster did not mention this point during his talks with the Director of Political and Commercial Affairs of the Foreign Ministry, Bargeton, yesterday. Fierce Fighting in the Rain Near Madrid; Government Troops Retreat to the Capital; Rebel General Offensive Also Delayed 72

San Juan de Torrués. The Spanish government forces and rebels are about to begin the battle for the capital, involving at least 200,000 people. Observers here believe today that this battle will be the only major battle since the European War, and the outcome will determine the fate of Spain. The rebel front now forms a semicircle from the Sierra de Guadarrama to Toledo. (National Telegraph, December 12th)

Madrid. Government troops and rebels are currently fighting fiercely in the rain 40 miles west of Madrid, striving to prevent the rebel advance. According to a government announcement, government troops have not conceded an inch of ground in this important area. Yesterday was the Spanish celebration of the anniversary of the discovery of the Americas. Originally, rebel commander-in-chief General Franco planned to launch a general offensive on the capital, but it seems to be postponed due to the government troops' counterattack and heavy rain. (Reuters, 13th)

Madrid. Rebel artillery and machine gun units were continuously transported to the Navalcarnero front line tonight. Believing that the rebels will attack at dawn, the Madrid government today prohibited foreign journalists from going to the front line to report on the war, the first time since the start of the war. According to government officials, this measure is intended to prevent the new offensive strategy from being leaked. (National Telegraph, December 12th)

Madrid. Government troops on the front line retreated to the capital today in preparation for a final defense. Government troops have launched partial counterattacks against the rebels in recent days, but due to the rebels' large numbers, advanced equipment, and well-trained officers, no significant progress has been made. Government troops are now hoping for drastic changes in the weather or the Soviet Union's withdrawal from the non-intervention agreement, so that they can purchase weapons from them. As for the rebels, they are advancing northward from Toledo, and their main forces will probably attack Navalcarnero and Illescas. The authorities here are on high alert for fascist plots. At the same time, the militia in the city, after days of street fighting with the rebels, recently occupied the Plaza de San Pedro. At present, most of the city is under artillery fire, and the militia is using bombs to destroy the rebel defenses. (Havas News Agency, 13th)

Madrid. The Ministry of Interior has recently issued an order that all bedding and winter clothing in houses and apartments in the capital whose residents are willing to live in the rebel-occupied areas and do not return to the capital will be confiscated and distributed to the army. This also applies to residents who have moved abroad since July 19th, the date of the rebellion. As for other houses and apartments still occupied by residents, each bed can retain one mattress and two quilts, and the rest must be handed over to the government for the use of the army, but the amount handed over will be registered, and the government will compensate for it in the future. Japan Develops North China's Economy: Mining Issues Settled in Two Steps; Li Szu-hao's Whereabouts Are Secret 75

Peiping Correspondence. The current focus of Sino-Japanese issues in North China is economic development, which includes mining, cotton planting, and the establishment of a transportation network. Currently, concrete negotiations have not been made on cotton planting and transportation. The mining issue has been decided. The first step is for the Hopei-Chahar Political Council to issue an order on the 12th to the Lungyen Iron Mine Company to expedite the settlement of matters. The council will order the Construction Committee to take the mine under state ownership. The second step is to conduct detailed exploration and planning. The Construction Committee is currently drafting a plan. It is likely that the mine will be jointly operated by Chinese and Japanese investment. The headquarters of the mine company will be located in Shihchingshan, west of Peiping. It has been closed for ten years, and the chimneys have rusted. The funds for repairs will be substantial. Funds are reportedly being raised. The mining area is located between Hsuanhua and Lungkuan in Chahar province. Since the establishment of the company, it has not been mined. It is decided that mining will resume immediately after the company takes over. Cotton planting and railway construction issues will be negotiated after the mining project is completed. Regarding the navigation issue, discussions were held once before, and opinions are being exchanged based on the original plan. However, because the views of both sides are still far apart, no concrete conclusions have been reached. In the past ten days, no further discussions have been held on this issue. As for the Hopei-Chahar Political Council, according to Japanese newspapers, a Standing Committee will be established with five members. This statement is indeed true. A few days ago, Sung Che-yuan invited key figures in Peiping, such as Chin Teh-chun, Chang Tzu-chung, and Liu Ju-ming, to exchange views several times at his private residence in the Wu-i-ku. He also visited Hsiao Chen-ying to discuss everything frankly. However, the selection of personnel to the Standing Committee requires considerable consideration. It is also difficult to predict whether the establishment of the Standing Committee will be more effective than the current one. If there is no such guarantee, then there is no need to establish it. It is now known that this issue has been temporarily shelved. As for Li Szu-hao's arrival in Peiping, there will be negotiations on the economic front. He has met with Sung several times. There is also a rumor that Li will succeed him as chairman of the Economic Committee. Li is currently staying at the Beijing Hotel and is refusing to see visitors. His whereabouts are very secretive. (12th)

Overview of Kwantung Leased Territory under Japanese Rule: Managed for Thirty Years as a Base for Aggression against Manchuria and Mongolia 76

Dairen Correspondence. The reason why the Japanese seized the Northeast is that they regard the South Manchuria Railway as their lifeline and the Kwantung Leased Territory as their base. Since the Sino-Japanese and Russo-Japanese Wars, the Kwantung Leased Territory has completely fallen under Japanese rule. All Japanese plans and aggressions against Manchuria and Mongolia are launched from the Kwantung Leased Territory. The September 18th Incident is one example. Now that the Northeast has been lost for five years, the Japanese have ruled the Kwantung Leased Territory for thirty years. The current situation in the territory is completely Japanized. The population, industry, and other conditions in the territory are recorded below for the information of the people of the country.

Population

The population of the Kwantung Leased Territory, according to a survey conducted by the Japanese last year (Japanese Showa 10th year), was 1,134,074. Of these, 163,796 were Japanese, 4,389 were Koreans, 963,875 were Chinese, and 204 were foreigners. Compared with the survey thirty years ago (Japanese Meiji 38th year), the population was 374,785, of which 5,035 were Japanese, 369,726 were Chinese, and 34 were foreigners. Under this comparison, the total population has almost tripled, and the Japanese population has increased by more than 34 times. The Chinese population has only increased by more than two times.

Agriculture and Animal Husbandry

The main agricultural products since Japanese rule are peanuts and fruit trees. The area planted with peanuts is more than 34,000 chōbu, with a harvest of 4 million yuan. Most of it is exported. The area planted with fruit trees is more than 5,100 chōbu, with a harvest of 5.6 million kan, valued at 2.8 million yuan. The main fruit is apples. The harvest of young trees now growing is expected to be four times as much. As for cultivating cotton, it is an important industry in the Japanese national policy. After years of research by the Kwantung Agricultural Experiment Station, the early-maturing variety of upland cotton, "Kwanno No. 1," which is suitable for cultivation in the Kwantung Leased Territory and southern Manchuria, has been improved and is about to be completed. This variety will be popularized in the territory and southern Manchuria. Today, the domestic poultry in the territory is heavily promoted and praised by the Japanese, who believe that it has become a superior breed. The improvement of pigs, cattle, and horses is particularly noticeable.

Salt Industry

The salt industry in the Kwantung Leased Territory is also the most distinctive and important industry. The climatic conditions of the Kwantung Leased Territory are suitable for sun-dried salt, and it can be manufactured anywhere along the coast. It has been a salt-producing area since ancient times. Later, at the beginning of Japanese rule, the scale was not large. There were 1,200 chōbu of Chinese salt fields. According to the Japanese, it has now reached more than 8,650 chōbu (90% of which are operated by the Japanese). As for the amount of salt produced, last year (Japanese Showa 10th year) the harvest reached 840 million catties, which is a production of 470,000 tons.

Industry and Commerce

Among the industries in the Kwantung Leased Territory, the ones with medium output are yarn, hemp bags, cement, glass, soybean oil, and lumber. According to the statistics of factories at the end of Showa 8th year (Japanese), (those employing more than five workers) there were 557 factories, with a total capital of more than 72 million yuan, and an annual output value of 69 million yuan.

Fishery

The Kwantung Leased Territory is surrounded by the sea on three sides, and the coastline is more than 700 miles long. There are more than 40 islands of various sizes, and the coast is rich in bays, making it convenient for boats. Fish production is abundant. According to its history, in September of the Japanese Meiji 38th year, as a result of the Russo-Japanese War, the Kwantung Leased Territory became a forced leasehold of the Japanese Empire. Therefore, many Japanese people moved into the Russian properties, so the demand for fish increased sharply. At that time, there were no fewer than 1,300 Japanese people who supplied fish for this purpose throughout the year. According to Japanese officials, the number of Japanese people accustomed to fishing has increased. Since 1925 (Japanese Taisho 14th year), when Japanese domestic motorized vessels aiming at the sea bream industry began large-scale bottom trawling in the Bohai and Longkou Straits, Japanese fishing now accounts for 80% based on this fishing method. Now, looking at the comparison of aquatic products between Meiji 39th year and Showa 8th year since the lease of the Kwantung Leased Territory, we can see its progress. (Fishery catch is in kan)

Japanese Meiji 39th year 375,538

Japanese Showa 8th year 13,520,000

Japanese fishermen use Dairen and Lushun as bases, and the islands near the sea, which are 700 miles from each other, are generally used as fishing grounds. Haiyang Island, famous for the Sino-Japanese War, is located at the eastern end of the Changshan Islands and has a natural harbor. It is now the base for fishermen. The important aquatic species are sea bream, cod, hairtail, flatfish, sea bass, mullet, mackerel, eel, conger eel, sea bass, and dozens of other species. In addition, the guidance of the Kwantung Leased Territory for the aquatic products industry is also very complete.

Anhui Highway Construction Status: Over 5,000 Kilometers of Highways Have Been Completed and Opened to Traffic; Railways Connect Chekiang-Kiangsi, Peiping-Hankow, Peiping-Canton, and Peiping-Pukow 77

Wuhu Correspondence. In addition to the trunk and branch roads determined by the Three Provinces Highway Conference and the Seven Provinces Highway Conference, and the provincial, county, and township connecting routes set by the province itself, Anhui province is also actively expanding trunk roads. At present, the province has 1,300 kilometers of paved highways and 4,000 kilometers of dirt roads open to traffic. In southern Anhui, there are the Wuhu-Tunxi, Hsuancheng-Changxing, Hangzhou-Huizhou, Sheng-Ying, Gu-Tunxi, Ching-Chien, Chun-Tunxi, and Tunxi-Chingde highways. Except for Nanling, Chingte, Tungling, and Fanchang counties, all other counties have direct or indirect connections with the trunk roads. The province is now supervising the above five counties to expedite the construction of county roads to facilitate connections. The important trunk roads in central Anhui include the Anqing-Hofei, Hofei-Liuan, Hofei-Chaoxian, Shu-Liuan, Kao-Chien, and Chien-Tai highways. Limited by financial resources, there are many dirt roads open to traffic in northern Anhui, which can directly reach Jiangsu and Henan provinces. Plans are underway to add paved surfaces and repair related routes to facilitate widespread connections. In addition, a section of the important Kueisui trunk road in northern Anhui is being paved and prepared for opening to traffic. In the future, from Hao County in northern Anhui, via the Kueisui road to Fuyang, then to Liuan, connecting with Liuhe, An-Hofei, Sheng-Tunxi, and Tun-Chi highways, it will be possible to reach Chi-men in southern Anhui and reach the Kiangsi province, completing a major trunk road running through the entire province from north to south. The important routes belonging to western Anhui include the Liu-Yeh, Liu-Huo, Huo-Yeh, Huo-Chu, Ta-Ma, and Ma-Liu highways, which can be used to reach Henan province directly. As for the Ching-Wu highway in eastern Anhui, because it has been open to traffic for several years, the ones currently being expedited include the Chu-Liu, Yu-Chiang, Ming-Chiang, Chuan-Pu, Tan-Lai, and Ho-Wu highways. After some time, the entire project will be completed. The railways in Anhui province are divided into three types: state-owned, provincial, and commercially operated. In the past, the only state-owned railway passing through the province was the Peiping-Pukow Railway, which facilitated foreign trade and transportation in Pengpu and Fengyang in northern Anhui. The provincial and commercially operated railways have only started in the past two or three years. For example, the Chiangnan Railway Company, which is commercially operated, completed the Ching-Sun section (170 kilometers long) last year. After it opened to traffic, inland transportation in Anhui province could directly reach Nanking and connect with the Peiping-Shanghai-Hangchow-Ningpo, and Peiping-Pukow, Lunghai, Peiping-Hankow, and Chiaochow-Tsinan Railways. Therefore, this year, the Ministry of Railways started to connect the Ching-Sun section of Chiangnan from Hsuancheng Sunchiapu, and built the Ching-Chi Railway, running through the counties of southern Anhui to Kweiki in Kiangsi, and connecting with the Chekiang-Kiangsi Railway and the Canton-Hankow Railway. There are now tens of thousands of workers starting construction from the provinces of Anhui and Kiangsi, and the survey work in Anhui has progressed from Hsuancheng beyond Ningkuo County towards the Hui district, reaching Chingtechen in Kiangsi. The total length of the entire route is 500 kilometers. The general engineering bureau is located in Hsuancheng. According to the director, Cheng Hua-yun, the entire route can be completed and opened to traffic by the end of next year. Also, the Huainan Railway of the state-owned Huainan Coal Mine Bureau, which is 220 kilometers long, has been completed and opened to traffic. It passes from the Tienchiuan mining area in Huaiyuan, western Anhui, through Hofei, Chaoxian, and Hanshan to Yuchiukou across the river from Wuhu. All sectors in the town of Changchiang utilized it, because the town originally belonged to an important town in western Anhui. The railroad transportation is crucial to the prosperity of rural commerce. The town is only ten kilometers away from Tienchiuan, so it has submitted a request to the Huainan Mining Bureau to extend it slightly and reach the town directly. However, the state-owned railway has its own fixed plan, which is not easy to change. Therefore, it was decided that the railway bureau would assist in the surveying and planning, and the merchants and residents of the town would raise funds and build it themselves. As for the ones that Anhui province plans to build, there is the section from Hofei to Yehchiachi of the Hsinyang-Pukow Railway. The road extends westward through Hsinyang in Henan and connects with the Peiping-Hankow Railway. Extending it southward from Hofei can reach Luochuan Town in Huaiyuan, Anhui, so that it can connect with the Huainan Railway. If it can be extended by another hundred miles, it can be connected to the Peiping-Pukow and Peiping-Hankow Railways and directly reach the capital. However, the construction cost is very large. There was a proposal for the central government to provide 8 million yuan and the provinces of Anhui and Henan to each raise 4 million yuan, so Anhui province is currently negotiating with the central government and the Henan provincial authorities to plan to start work as soon as possible. (12th)

Sungkiang 79

Robbery at Lung-hsing Yehchia-wei

At about 11:00 p.m. on the 12th, the home of Yeh Chin-liang, a farmer in the 7th bao, 5th chia, and 4th household of Lung-hsing Village, District 1, was visited by seven or eight bandits speaking a northern Kiangsu dialect. Each held pistols, sharp knives, ropes, candles, etc. They broke the back door and entered, tying up all the men and women in the Yeh family. Only Chin-liang hid behind the back door and was not tied up. He went out the back door to call for help, but was quickly shot twice by the bandit guarding the door, hitting his right leg. One bullet went through, and one did not, causing him to bleed and fall to the ground. The bandits whistled and fled east. After the victim inspected the losses, it was found that Yeh's mother, Shen, was robbed of 20 yuan, and his sister-in-law, Wang, was robbed of 50 yuan. Before leaving, the bandits carelessly dropped a sharp knife, a hemp rope, and two pairs of shoes. The victim reported the incident to the Second Police Station on the morning of the 13th to pursue the bandits. It was heard that when the bandits fled, they robbed Yeh's small ferry boat. It was not discovered until dawn in the Kuantang River, about half a mile away.

Changshu 80

Red Cross Branch Organizes Malaria Eradication Team

This autumn, malaria has been found to be very serious in the eastern townships of this county, with successive deaths. Some people even die within three to five days, and it is spreading very rapidly and is everywhere. According to the statistics report of the district office, on average, one person in every two households suffers from this disease, which is a serious situation. However, the villagers are misled by superstition, do not seek fundamental treatment, and turn to the superstition of ghosts and gods, so the situation is not alleviated. The local Red Cross branch, seeing the rampant malaria in the township, plans to organize a malaria eradication team. It will depart soon with doctors from the local Western Medical Association to various areas, either to provide injections or to donate quinine pills, so that the malaria germs can be eradicated as soon as possible.

The Ministry of Justice has decided to establish county courts in the four counties of Kiangyin, Changshu, Taishing, and Ju-kao in Kiangsu Province, and to establish them within the next three months. Random Talks on Rural Life 84

— Edited by Yu Qingtang

The Rural Sentinel Station in Taixing (Part 2) Qi Feng

What I personally experienced in my hometown during my summer vacation was like this. According to my family members, in addition to unclear and inexplicable extortion from the villagers, they openly established many forms of exploitation, leaving the common people in a state of mixed emotions. For example, birthday fundraising is a very obvious example. I heard that there are countless people in my hometown celebrating birthdays every year. The township head wants to celebrate his birthday, the bao head wants to celebrate his birthday, and the guo dong wants to celebrate his birthday. Among them, the "Bureau Chief" seems to celebrate birthdays the most diligently and profitably. The "Bureau Chief" celebrates birthdays at least three or four times a year. After celebrating his own birthday, he celebrates his son's birthday. After his son's birthday, he celebrates the death anniversary of his mother, who died twenty years ago. When the "Bureau Chief" celebrates a birthday, he does not wait for people to voluntarily come to congratulate him. Instead, the baojia leaders are required to distribute congratulatory gifts from village to village. Each birthday celebration brings in at least five or six hundred yuan! In addition to celebrating birthdays to raise money, there is also the firearms donation, and after the firearms donation, there is the winter defense donation. The winter defense donation happens every year, costing five hundred yuan each time. How can the poor farmers afford such exorbitant taxes?

As soon as the summer vacation ended, I went to another village. Regarding the various virtuous policies of the sentinel station, I didn't know as many details as when I was at home, except for occasionally seeing one or two records in the newspaper. Recently, a letter from home said that our "Bureau Chief" had committed treason and was arrested by the county government and taken to Zhenjiang. It also said that on the day the "Bureau Chief" was arrested and taken to the city, the "Bureau Chief's" followers caused a great disturbance. They were deeply afraid that the "Bureau Chief" would never return, so they threatened many villagers in various villages to put down their hoes and help them petition in the city. Although the villagers were happy that there was one less bad person in the area, they had to follow to the city under the threat of these partisans. More than seven hundred people crammed into the City God Temple, starving for most of the day. Later, they didn't hear any news, and one by one, they secretly fled back.

What I have said above is entirely about the situation of the sentinel station in my hometown. As for whether the sentinel stations in other places are also like this, I dare not say. However, in a local newspaper in a certain county in Jiangbei in September, I saw a notice stating that "Recently, it has been heard that some sentinel stations in various villages have privately lent firearms to bandits for robbery, which is extremely illegal..." It can be seen that it is similar to what happens in my hometown. As for whether the sentinel station has corrected itself after receiving this solemn notice, the following two news items can answer that question.

1. Fu Xiang, the abbot of the God of Wealth Temple in Du Ju Township, Fifth District, had a godson, Dai Yushou, from the Guanjiazhuang Village in Zhang Feng Township of the same district, two years ago. Therefore, the monk introduced Yushou to study at the Dujiazhuang Elementary School. At the end of last month, Yushou went home due to some matters and did not go to school for many days. The principal of the school, Ye Rongbin, immediately asked the monk to urge him to return. As soon as he arrived at Yushou's home, a heavy rain suddenly fell, preventing him from returning. The sentinel station's Ding Guan Tai and Xiao Zhengxin and others went to Yushou's house with guns. They claimed that a stranger had come to his home, and why had he not reported it to the bao head? They said that he must be severely punished. They fired two shots to intimidate him in every possible way. Later, after the Bao head Ken Yingguang and villagers Xiao Yingshu and others mediated, Dai Yushou wrote a ten-yuan voucher before they were released.

2. Xiao Decan from Xiaowan Village, Gengdai Township, First District, was addicted to smoking opium. Yesterday, he sent his daughter Zhennv to the city to buy tobacco. On her way home, she passed the Fangjiazhuang Sentinel Station and was suddenly robbed of ten yuan by a strongman. Zhennv was too young to resist, so she cried and went home.

I don't want to write any more about the illegal actions of our Jiangbei sentinel stations. The purpose of establishing sentinel stations, as the name suggests, is to have them assist and protect the villages. Now, not only can they not help and protect the villages, but they have also become an agency that extorts and exploits the people. What else is there to say? Some people say that the reason why the Jiangbei sentinel stations are so harmful to the local area is due to three reasons: First, the director is not a proper person; second, the sentinel station workers are not local farmers; and third, the sentinel station workers only receive three yuan a month, which is too little pay. We also agree with this. However, the reason why the sentinel station is organized in this way is still caused by the local feudal forces. We believe that the local feudal forces are a source of disaster, and the sentinel station is just one manifestation of this source of disaster. If the root of the disaster is not removed, the sentinel station will forever become a tool for exploiting the masses of farmers!

Note 1: "Bureau Chief" is the term used by farmers to refer to the director of the sentinel station. The director often calls himself "Bureau Chief."

Note 2: "Smoke Lamp" is the common name used by farmers for opium smoking dens.

Zhang Xian's Posthumous Exhibition Opens Today 90

The late painter Zhang Xian had studied in France twice. Throughout his life, he devoted himself to art tirelessly for twenty years. His recent works, including line drawings of ladies and oil paintings of landscapes, are particularly moving in their lines and colors and have a unique style. Unfortunately, he was talented but short-lived, and died with unfulfilled ambitions. His friends have selected more than 300 fine works from Zhang's more than 2,000 posthumous works and are holding a public exhibition for five days in the hall on the fourth floor of the Daxin Company. Mr. Cai Jiemin will personally hold the opening ceremony this afternoon. It is also heard that all proceeds from the sale of paintings at this decision exhibition will be allocated to the education and upbringing fund for his orphans.

Situation of Students Studying in the U.S. Arriving Safely in Seattle 91

Among the Chinese students studying in the United States over the years, the number of students passing through Seattle to land is the largest this year. There were four major groups arriving in September, including 52 people on the Grand President of the Dollar Steamship Company on the 2nd, 87 people on the Empress of Japan of the Shipia Steamship Company on the 8th, 40 people on the President Jefferson on the 16th, and 30 people on the Empress of Asia on the 21st, totaling 214 people. Prior to this, the Consul in Seattle, Lu Shiyin, contacted the US Immigration Bureau, Customs and other authorities, and went to Victoria to secretly explain the procedures for dealing with immigration and customs inspections of luggage and passports, in order to avoid unexpected problems. In order to facilitate the students' landing and save time, Consul Lu also requested the Immigration Bureau to send personnel to Victoria to check passports on the ship. The students all felt convenient, and no one was detained. After landing, Consul Lu accompanied them to the Madeng Hostel opened by overseas Chinese for rest. The owner of the hostel offered preferential rates for students, with rent of only 2.5 jiao per person. After the students arrived, the Consul also specially prepared tea and snacks to entertain them. Consul Lu also consulted with the Chinese Rotary Club, the Zhongsu Association, the City Chamber of Commerce and other organizations to host banquets for the first and second groups of students and invite them to visit various scenic spots. Afterwards, the students sent letters of thanks. The consulate said.

Sports News

International Football Association Notice - Several Changes to the Football Rules - National Sports Federation Translates and Announces - Decided to Officially Adopt from This Season 95

The International Football Association has decided on several changes to the football rules this year. The Chinese National Sports Federation has received the association's official notice and decided to officially adopt them from this season. The changes are translated and explained as follows:

After the first sentence of Article 1 of Chapter 7, add the words "Directly kick out of the penalty area." The full sentence reads as follows:

If the ball is kicked over the end line by a player of the opposing team, any player of the team to which that end of the goal belongs shall place the ball within the goal area closer to where it went out of bounds and kick it directly out of the penalty area, which is called a goal kick.

(Referee's Note) When taking a goal kick, the goalkeeper shall not use the example of holding a ball kicked up by a teammate with his hand and then kicking it out again.

The goal kick must be kicked directly out of the penalty area from within the goal area. If the ball fails to kick out of the penalty area, it shall be retaken.

Add the words "between the two goalposts" to the first sentence of Chapter 10. The full sentence reads as follows:

When taking a free kick, the players of the opposing team, except those standing on the end line between the two goalposts of their own side, shall not stand within a radius of ten yards from the ball before the ball is kicked out.

(Note) The above sentence is only a revision of the wording, and the meaning of the text has not changed.

The first sentence of Chapter 12 is changed as follows:

The iron nails used on the players' football shoes must be nailed into the leather, and the players shall not wear football shoes or shin guards with metal plates or other protrusions or rubber.

(Old Rule) Players shall not wear football shoes or shin guards with nails (excluding those with nail heads exposed on the leather) or metal plates, or other protrusions or rubber.

(Note) This article is only a revision of the wording, and the meaning of the text has not changed.

The Guiding Principles of Physical Education for National Revival 99

— Wu Cheng

Address at the Opening Ceremony of the Shanghai Municipal School of Physical Education on October 12th

(Central News Agency) Distinguished guests, fellow students, today is the opening ceremony of the Shanghai Municipal School of Physical Education. I am deeply honored to serve concurrently as the principal of this school.

The reason why the Shanghai Municipal Government decided to establish this school of physical education is that its purpose is profound and far-reaching. Although the financial situation of Shanghai is currently very strained, why did we resolutely decide to establish this specialized physical education school under such circumstances? I had this idea a long time ago. When the Shanghai Municipal Government planned to build a sports field, I already had this idea, which was to attach a physical education school to the sports field to make full use of this large sports field. Because this sports field is not only the largest in China, but also the largest in the Far East to date. Since we have built such a large sports field, we cannot leave it empty and unused. Moreover, it will be more convenient to run a physical education school attached to such a magnificent and relatively well-equipped sports field in the future. Therefore, when the Municipal Government built the sports field two years ago, I already had this idea. But why is this physical education school only being established today? The first is the issue of funding, and the second is the situation. Today's economy is, of course, still as difficult as before, and today's situation is not necessarily better than before. So why are we resolutely establishing this physical education school today? There is a major impetus, which is the decision of the Chinese delegation to participate in the World Games, which caused us the greatest shame and gave us the greatest lesson. What we consider shameful is not because the Chinese delegation did not get any points, but because our physique is so far behind compared with those of other countries in the world that it cannot be measured by miles. This can indeed be said to be the hidden worry of China's national subjugation and racial extinction. Even without external troubles, if the physique of our people continues to decline, our nation will not be able to compete with others and will not be able to survive in today's fiercely competitive world. This has given us the greatest stimulus, so we disregard everything. No matter how difficult the finances are or how bad the situation is, we still resolutely establish this physical education school.

Our physical education school has its own unique spirit. The common misconception among people is that the purpose of running a physical education school is to train athletes to promote the school. This view is very wrong and very dangerous. The reason why we promote physical education is not simply to train athletes, let alone to run a physical education school only for participating in sports meets. We must use various methods and aspects to forge a healthy physique so that the physique of the whole nation can be equally healthy. After the physique of the whole nation is healthy, we will select outstanding athletes from the healthy physique of the whole nation to participate in sports meets. It is definitely not putting the cart before the horse to train athletes just for participating in sports meets. Moreover, strictly speaking, our athletes should be selected from people of any occupation in the country. Only athletes produced in this way can truly represent such a powerful nation. Therefore, we must vigorously correct the current wrong physical education policy, because the greatest purpose of our promoting physical education is to forge a healthy physique for every individual of the whole nation, so that the people can use their healthy physique to engage in their respective careers and have the confidence to succeed in their careers. If the physique of every member of the nation is healthy and their careers can be successful, then why should the entire nation worry about not being able to revive and develop? Foreigners often ridicule us Chinese as "sick men of East Asia." Why do foreigners ridicule us Chinese as "sick men of East Asia"? Why do we not know shame or strive to improve after being ridiculed by others? Because we have never been able to see clearly where our illness lies. In ancient China, both literature and martial arts were equally emphasized, so hunting and reading were equally important, and horsemanship and music were equally valued. After the Song Dynasty, the six arts were completely abandoned, and people specialized in studying and annotating texts. Since then, a trend of valuing literature over martial arts has developed, and the physique of the people has declined day by day, so they are called "sick men of East Asia." But we ourselves do not know where our illness lies, which is really dangerous. People with superficial views believe that China lacks a strong navy, a sophisticated air force, modern artillery, and strong fortresses, so it is called "sick men of East Asia." Therefore, they demand that the government expand its military equipment every day to resist foreign insults. Of course, military equipment is very important, but can airplanes fly by themselves? Can warships sail by themselves? Can military equipment and fortresses fully exert their combat capabilities by themselves? These all require people to drive and use them, but where are the people? Can people with weak and unhealthy physiques drive them? Will they have the spirit and courage to endure hardship and command? Therefore, if people's physiques are not healthy, airplanes, warships, and artillery are useless. Now, most of our people are still not ashamed of being called "sick men of East Asia," and they still do not know how to strive for improvement or how to extricate themselves, which is a great hidden worry for the nation. President Chiang Kai-shek is worried about this, so he wants to promote the New Life Movement to stimulate the spirit of the people across the country and fundamentally remove the name of "sick man of East Asia." Now, the lives of our people fully display morbidities such as arrogance, complacency, laziness, cowardice, sloppiness, disorder, self-abandonment, and selfishness. How can a nation living like this not be weak, not perish, and not be bullied by others? The most important and fundamental work of implementing the New Life Movement should start with physical education, because the Ministry of Education stipulates that the goal of physical education is to cultivate various virtues such as obedience, endurance, self-government, courage, unity, mutual assistance, and discipline. If we can cultivate the virtue of obedience, we can sweep away the past morbidity of arrogance. If we can cultivate the virtue of endurance, we can sweep away the past morbidity of complacency and laziness. If we can cultivate the virtue of self-government, we can sweep away the past morbidity of self-abandonment. If we can cultivate the virtue of courage, we can sweep away the past morbidity of cowardice. If we can cultivate the virtue of mutual assistance, we can sweep away the past morbidity of selfishness. If we can cultivate the virtue of discipline, we can sweep away the past morbidity of disorder. In short, we must eradicate all the morbidities of the past and replace them with virtues such as obedience, endurance, self-government, courage, unity, mutual assistance, and discipline. If every member of our nation possesses these virtues, our nation will surely be able to revive quickly. This is the highest goal of our physical education. In addition, what you should pay attention to is that physical education in the future should be integrated with military affairs. After the European War, the physical education policies of various countries are different from before. Their teaching materials and methods all emphasize stimulating the spirit of the people to struggle. In addition to strengthening the physical and mental health of young people and the people, they also have the purpose of incorporating military training into physical education. For example, Italy regards physical education as an urgent task for national revival. For example, the Soviet Union regards sports meets as a "production and national defense examination" for the people across the country. Therefore, the establishment of our school is not just to train a few excellent athletes, but to train teachers who integrate physical education and military affairs, and to further seek to popularize physical education among the people so that the people across the country can have healthy physiques. We hope that our school can become a center for mass physical education in the future. After the opening of school today, I hope that the principal, faculty, and all students will thoroughly understand the government's intention in establishing this school, recognize our goals, and work together to fulfill its mission. (End)

Overview of Shanghai Japanese Schools (8) Special Report from This Newspaper 101

— Investigation by Hu Zuyin

(10) Sports Facilities Japanese schools pay great attention to the physical and mental development of children. Therefore, all schools are actively engaged in the construction of sports facilities and spare no effort. The sports facilities of each school are mostly complete. The area of the school's sports field is very large. Several schools also have gyms and covered playgrounds. The Japanese Higher Girls' School, completed in Yun Sui, also has a newly built indoor swimming pool. The Japanese Central Ordinary Elementary School is currently working on building an elementary school swimming pool, which will be completed soon.

Each school has sufficient sports equipment and apparatus. Now, let's list the sports equipment and apparatus equipped by the Central Ordinary Elementary School as a representative to show a glimpse of it. The school is equipped with 30 sets of wall bars, 5 sets of horizontal bars, 3 sets of vaulting boxes, 5 sets of high and low platforms, basketball hoops, volleyball hoops, 5 sets of balance beams, 4 sets of springboards, 3 sets of mats, 5 sets of low iron bars, 2 sets of parallel bars, 2 sets of high jump equipment, 1 set of baseball equipment, 50 gymnastic short benches, and dozens of various sizes of leather balls.

Each school has a health room: All kinds of equipment for first aid, disinfection and cleaning, physical examination, and treatment of trachoma are completely purchased. There are also devices for corridor insulation, dust prevention in classrooms, and watering the playground. There are also hand washing and foot washing areas for children to wash their hands and feet after exercise.

Regarding the issue of physical education teaching, the school has also compiled a book entitled "Attitude towards Guiding Physical Exercise," which fully explains their views on physical education teaching. Now, let's excerpt and introduce the points to note in guiding children's physical education in each grade from the book:

(1) Points to note when guiding physical education for lower grade children:

(1) Emphasize natural exercise, (2) Guide children's games well, (3) Inspire children's designed activities, (4) Develop children's free activities, (5) Pay attention to the use of children's whole body muscles, (6) Emphasize children's imaginative and imitative activities, (7) Cultivate children's interest in physical education, (8) Pay attention to children's impulsive emotions.

(2) Points to note when guiding physical education for middle grade children:

(1) Gymnasticize natural exercise, (2) Enhance the development function of various parts of the body, (3) Thoroughly practice basic exercises, (4) Train children's nervous system, (5) Emphasize social training, (6) Cultivate children's sentiments, (7) Pay attention to children's active period.

(3) Points to note when guiding physical education for upper grade children: (1) Cultivate children's awareness of physical education, (2) Fully develop the functions of various parts of the body, (3) Actively train the body, (4) Train the nervous system, (5) Cultivate the spirit of competition, (6) Cultivate the attitude of Taiwan cooperation, (7) Cultivate physical education interest and physical education knowledge, (8) Adapt to personality, (9) Pay attention to children's sentiments.

(4) Points to note when guiding girls' physical education:

(1) Emphasize pleasant and balanced exercise, (2) Emphasize free exercise and games, (3) Have more trunk exercise to cultivate graceful posture, (4) Develop the functions of various parts of the body, (5) Increase the amount of basic teaching materials and reduce the amount of applied teaching materials, (6) Have more marching and rhythmic exercise, (7) Avoid strenuous exercise, (8) Inverted and turning exercises are unnecessary, (9) Emphasize game teaching materials that can express emotions, (10) Pay attention to appropriate rest and recuperation.

Ningbo Association for Purchasing and Preparing Grain Reached Agreement Yesterday 110

After Yu Qiaqing and other leaders of the Ningbo Chamber of Commerce in Shanghai initiated the purchase and preparation of grain, they discussed the methods at the Ningbo Fellow Villagers Association at 4 pm yesterday and decided to organize the Ningbo Association for Purchasing and Preparing Grain to prepare to purchase and prepare grain worth 1.5 million yuan. The required advance payment of 300,000 yuan will be jointly recognized by the members of the Association. The details are recorded as follows:

Decision-Making Method

A meeting was held at the Ningbo Fellow Villagers Association at 4 pm yesterday, with Qin Runqing, Fu Bian, Yu Qiaqing, Zhu Meiguang, Sun Hengfu, Yu Zuoting, Jin Tingsun, Xu Shengchan, Yue Zhenbao, Zhang Jiyao, Fang Jiaobo, Mao Heyuan, and others. Yu Qiaqing chaired the meeting and reported the purpose of purchasing and preparing grain. The following methods were discussed and agreed upon: (1) The quantity of grain to be purchased and prepared is estimated at 1.5 million national currency; (2) The purchased grain will be mortgaged to the bank (not yet determined), and the interest (not yet determined) will be guaranteed by the provincial government; (3) In addition to mortgaging the grain, an advance payment of 300,000 yuan will be required, which will be borrowed from a certain bank by the members of the Association, and each member will be responsible for the amount they borrow, and the interest will be officially set at (not yet determined); (4) If there is a loss after the grain is sold, the provincial government and the advance payer will each bear half of the loss, which will be settled in their advance payment.

Jointly Recognizing Advance Payment

The amount of 300,000 yuan to be paid in advance was recognized on the spot, including Yu Qiaqing 5,000 yuan, Xu Shengchan 5,000 yuan, Zhang Jiyao 5,000 yuan, Yue Zhenbao 5,000 yuan, Jin Tingsun 5,000 yuan, Fu Xiao'an 5,000 yuan, Yu Zuoting 5,000 yuan, Sun Hengfu 5,000 yuan, Mao Heyuan 5,000 yuan, Zhu Meixian 5,000 yuan, Qin Runqing 5,000 yuan, Fang Jiaobo 5,000 yuan, Zhan Yuan 5,000 yuan, totaling 65,000 yuan, and the remaining 235,000 yuan was decided to be raised from fellow villagers in Shanghai.

Letter Requesting Signature and Recognition

The Association sent letters to fellow villagers in Shanghai yesterday requesting signature and recognition of the advance payment, "Sir, because the counties of Ningbo have always lacked grain production and rely on imports from outside to distribute food to the people, it is insufficient. It is proposed to initiate the Ningbo Association for Purchasing and Preparing Grain to engage in preparation and first request the provincial government and consult with Zhejiang Farmers Bank to predetermine the methods as follows, (see above) In addition to the Association handling procedures with the provincial government and a certain bank, please also warmly support and sign as an advance payer, I am very grateful."

Social Affairs Bureau Petitions the City Government to Prohibit the Export of Our Country's Food, Ordering the Suppression of Soaring Food Prices and the Crackdown on Speculation; Various Trade Associations Voluntarily Refuse to Sell to Foreign Merchants, and Propose Measures to Regulate Domestic Food Supply and Transportation 111

According to the New Voice News Agency, the Shanghai Municipal Social Affairs Bureau, in order to stabilize the price of food for the people, instructed the Soybean and Rice Trade Association and others to prevent price increases, and reported to the Municipal Government, which forwarded the request to the Central Government to prohibit exports. Various food organizations have voluntarily prevented price increases and exports, and have proposed measures to restrict transportation to various regions. The details are as follows:

Prohibition of Exports

Since the Social Affairs Bureau convened a meeting of various food organizations to stabilize rice prices, in addition to instructing the Soybean and Rice Trade Association and other related organizations to prevent the increase in prices of rice, wheat, flour, etc., the bureau also submitted a report on the meeting's proceedings and the two stabilization measures decided upon by Director Pan Gongzhan to the Municipal Council meeting. At the same time, it reported to the Municipal Government, which forwarded the request to the Central Government to prohibit the export of rice, wheat, flour, etc., in order to maintain the food supply for the people. Meanwhile, the Food Supply Division of the Fourth Section of the bureau dispatched staff members to various locations to monitor the situation, and those who deliberately raised prices would be severely punished.

Suppressing Soaring Prices

Shanghai Municipal Social Affairs Bureau Instruction to the Soybean and Rice Trade Association and other organizations, Hai Zi No. 362, states: "It has been found that the recent surge in food prices has had a significant impact on the food supply for the residents of this city. According to investigation, this year's food harvest in various regions is abundant, and production has increased. Furthermore, the daily arrivals of goods have not decreased. At this time when new goods are entering the market, such a phenomenon should not occur. In order to protect the livelihood of the common people, this bureau cannot ignore the situation. In addition to dispatching personnel to thoroughly investigate any speculative manipulation, once verified, those responsible will be punished. The association is hereby ordered to comply and effectively suppress the soaring food prices in order to value the people's food supply. This order is issued."

Stabilizing Food Prices

A reporter from the New Voice News Agency visited Mr. Gu Xinyi, a leader in the grain industry, yesterday morning. According to him, since the Social Affairs Bureau convened various food organizations to discuss and decide on stabilization measures, the various trade associations of miscellaneous grains, soybeans, rice, etc., immediately instructed their members to stop raising food prices. Currently, food prices have fallen back, approximately 40 to 50 cents per dan lower than the highest point. The previous price increase was actually caused by rumors about the current situation. This is a temporary phenomenon because this year's late rice harvest in various regions of our country has been plentiful, and there is no concern about a shortage. Therefore, there is no reason for a surge in prices.

Trade Association Refusal

Furthermore, in order to prevent the export of our country's rice, wheat, flour, etc., various trade associations of miscellaneous grains, soybeans, and flour have voluntarily refused to sell to foreign merchants. For example, recently a certain merchant was procuring a large quantity of wheat in Shanghai, but because Chinese merchants refused to sell, they were unable to purchase it. As for the current prices of wheat and flour, they are higher than before because the prices of foreign wheat have risen, which has led to an increase in the price of domestic wheat.

Regulating the Food Supply

Furthermore, in order to regulate the domestic food supply and prevent exports, the grain industry advocates that if it is necessary to transport food out, it must be certified by the trade association, and a shipping permit must be issued before transportation is allowed. In the event of a period of short supply, the trade association may stop issuing shipping permits. This measure will be submitted by the trade association to the government authorities for approval, and so on.
