Two Native Place Associations Plead for the Salt Farmers of Daishan 115

Requesting Exemption from Returning Stacks and Color-Changing Salt for Fishery Use

Yu Qiaqing, Chairman of the Ningbo Native Place Association, and Liu Hongsheng, Chairman of the Dinghai Native Place Association, jointly telegraphed President Chiang yesterday, stating: "Respectfully submit this matter: Based on a letter jointly signed by salt farmer representatives Liu Linzhao, Chen Chifu, Tang Xinian, Chu Kaiyou, Yu Danqiu, Zou Renyi, Xia Jichang, Wang Shengzhao, Yu Mingshen, Wang Chuntang, Chen Xianglin, and Wu Moyou of Daishan salt farm, stating: 'Daishan is a solitary island surrounded by dozens of miles. There are many mud flats and few fields. There are more than 10,000 households with a population of over 70,000. 70-80% are engaged in salt production, and 20-30% are engaged in agriculture, fishing, and commerce. However, merchants from other regions are not included. The prosperity or decline of commerce depends on the abundance or scarcity of salt production. In recent years, there have been continuous poor harvests, and all industries have declined as a result. Therefore, the entire Daishan Island relies on the salt industry as its core. Recently, the Daishan Salt Farm Office has been handling the return of stacks and color-changing salt for fishery use. All our salt farmers should comply with this, but there are special circumstances in Daishan farm, which are different from those in Lianghuai, Changlu, Hedong, and other places. The representatives have no choice but to present the following information: It has been found that the Daishan produces salt in mud flats, totaling more than 25,000 mu. The current measurement of returning the base of the stack is more than 100 places, and the central mud flats have been divided into 400 to 500 mu. 5000 to 6000 mu of mud flats have been wasted out of thin air. If each family of several people has 50 drying boards and needs 5 to 6 mu of mud flats, there are still more than 1,000 families whose mud flats have been designated as stack bases, resulting in the loss of livelihood for thousands of salt farmers. Therefore, the return of the stack should be temporarily postponed. First, an investigation reveals that the cost of salt production is lowest in Qingdao and Fujian, because the seawater is salty and labor is saved. Compared with Daishan farm, the opposite is true. Daishan farm has excessively diluted seawater, and salt production requires more than 100 transfers of shoulder carrying to make the salt. Therefore, the cost is heavier than any other salt farm. If free trade is allowed in the future after the return of the stack, Daishan farm will inevitably be ignored, and Daishan farm will perish without being abolished. Therefore, the return of the stack should be temporarily postponed. Second, the return of the base of the stack has occupied more than one-fifth of the mud flats, and the annual salt production will be shorted by more than 110,000 dan (Daishan farm has 250,000 drying boards, and each board produces 4 dan of salt per year, totaling 1 million dan). Even in terms of taxation, at 7.1 yuan per dan, the tax revenue will be reduced by 1.5 million yuan. It seems that it is neither beneficial to the people nor necessarily beneficial to the country. Therefore, the return of the stack should be temporarily postponed. Third, after the stacks are completed, the salt farmers must return the salt to the stack at 4 PM. This is the normal office hour for various agencies and is not surprising. However, for salt farmers, this is the time when they are working hard and cannot be interrupted. Moreover, at the turn of summer and autumn, the stacking of salt (referring to stacking and gathering on drying cups) must be done at 6 or 7 PM. During these three hours, approximately 2 jin of salt can be produced, which is a direct loss to the salt farmers and an indirect loss to the national tax revenue. It is even more difficult to return the stacks after 7 PM, as both parties will be hungry and working for the public interest. Therefore, the return of the stack should be temporarily postponed. Fourth, as for the color-changing salt for fishery use, the intention is to crack down on smuggling, but genuine salt farmers are determined not to engage in smuggling. The reasons have been widely seen in various newspapers and do not need to be repeated. However, the harm of color-changing salt for fishery use and the great impact on fishing boats, fishing factories, fishing merchants, and various fishing industries will not be discussed here for the time being. Even the suffering of our salt farmers is already considerable, but the cost has increased and the procedures are cumbersome. One party prepares the harvest, and the other party prepares the sale. White salt cannot be stained red, and red salt cannot be added to white. The small houses are cramped, the utensils are dilapidated, and leaks are everywhere. The old and young sigh. Carrying a load of red salt to exchange for a liter of rice, they are worried about uneven mixing and violating the law. The state of their distress is difficult to describe. Reading the new salt law, the simple provisions regarding fishery salt are only in Articles 3, 5, and 25, and there is no clear text on color-changing salt for fishery use. Only industrial and agricultural salt is subject to denaturation and color change, but under Article 6, Paragraph 3 and Paragraph 6, the salt required may require the purchaser to provide a corresponding guarantee or collateral without denaturation or color change. This is the tax-free industrial salt that can be exempted from color change when necessary, but the fishery salt does not necessarily need to be changed. Why is this in the salt law? The denaturation or color change of salt is carried out by the salt quality inspector in the warehouse. Now, the salt farmers are ordered to do it themselves, which often leads to mistakes, which is not unfair. Therefore, the exemption of color-changing salt for fishery use should be requested. Fifth, Daishan is the second largest farm in Zhejiang, with a large output. The food for the people and the national tax revenue are very important. Of course, it is not included in the list of abolition and merger. Moreover, our salt farmers are concerned with life and death and are deeply affected. They have no choice but to weep and appeal, and directly state the advantages and disadvantages. We hope that your association will consider the circumstances and plead on their behalf. The return of salt stacks should be temporarily postponed, and the color change of fishery salt should be exempted in order to maintain the livelihood and relieve the suffering of the people. ' etc. After investigating the salt farmers' statements, there are indeed various difficulties. According to the above, the above situation is specially forwarded to your office for review and approval, and we hope that you will consider the suffering of the salt farmers and promptly order the Ministry of Finance and the Salt Affairs Administration to handle it carefully in order to relieve the suffering of the people."

Tea Association Annual Meeting Disrupted and Suspended Yesterday Due to Membership Eligibility Issues; Mediation Approaches and Resumption of Discussions Possible Today 117

According to the Central News Agency, the Second General Meeting of the First Annual Conference of the China Tea Association, which was the third day yesterday, was held at Lake Society starting at 9 AM. More than 100 people, including all members and representatives from the construction departments of various provinces, attended the Second General Meeting. After the meeting began, a misunderstanding arose over the eligibility of new members, which prevented the meeting from proceeding according to the original agenda. Representatives of the Municipal Party Department, Mao Yun, and the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau, Wu Huanru, attended and mediated after consultation, asking both parties to abandon their prejudices, take into account the articles of association and the facts, and jointly discuss appropriate solutions. Tea is an important trade in our country, and it is hoped that they will focus on the business, cooperate with each other, etc. Subsequently, the presidium announced the adjournment of the meeting and will notify a new date for the meeting. They dispersed unhappily around 11 AM.

Reasons for the Dispute

According to the reporter's investigation, the dispute at this meeting was indeed due to the eligibility of new members, but in essence, it was a conflict between politics and business. When the association was established, there were only 20-odd members, and the nature of its organization focused on technical research. At this conference, the number of people who registered and joined the association increased to more than 100. They were quite dissatisfied with the government's policy on the marketing of black tea in recent years and intended to designate a motion in the association to oppose it. Therefore, the occurrence of the problem eventually formed a conflict between politics and business.

Meeting Suspension

According to the association's articles of association, new members can only become members after being introduced by two members and approved by the board of directors. More than 100 people joined at the same time this time. Due to the board of directors' negligence, they were not reviewed. During the first discussion, all members present voted, and new members were also nominated as review committee members. Subsequently, the board of directors saw that an unexpected change was about to occur and invoked the articles of association as a remedy, but were criticized by the new members, causing the meeting to be suspended.

Mediation Approaches

After the board of directors held a meeting first yesterday afternoon, representatives of the Municipal Party Department, Mao Yun, and the Social Affairs Bureau, Wu Huanru, invited the board of directors and one representative from each region to participate and mediate tactfully, asking them to focus on the business and release their emotional disputes. According to the results released, both parties have gradually approached an agreement and have scheduled to continue the meeting today, and it is expected that the General Meeting will be reopened tomorrow.

Municipal Chamber of Commerce Telegraphs Ministry of Finance Requesting Exemption from Inspecting Western Medicines 120

The Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce telegraphed the Ministry of Finance yesterday, stating: "Nanjing Ministry of Finance: It is hereby requested that the Ministry of Finance issue an order to the Shanghai New Medicine Trade Association stating that the types of imported goods inspected by the Ministry of Finance at the beginning did not include Western medicines and that Western medicines should not be included in the types of imported goods inspected, etc. After investigation, the items listed in the amended types of imported goods to be inspected include both Chinese and Western medicines. There are as many as 50,000 to 60,000 types of items, and Japanese goods only account for one-tenth, which is less than Chinese medicines. Even if there is a fear of smuggling, several types should be designated as inspection standards, so that both officials and merchants can feel convenient in handling matters, and it is more conducive to preventing smuggling. If the category of medicines is included in a general way, the scope is too broad, which is not only difficult for merchants to handle, but also causes unnecessary work for anti-smuggling agencies. It has been found that the union has established an anti-smuggling branch, and has made considerable preparations for preventing smuggling work. There is absolutely no possibility of smuggled goods being active. The request to exempt Western medicines from being included in the types of imported goods to be inspected is not excessive. We hereby telegraph the Ministry to review and approve the request, which is for the public good. The Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce respectfully presents this matter."

Datong Company's Yongsheng Ship Runs Aground Off Quanzhou 121

Has Been Rescued, Freed and Arrived in Quanzhou The Datong Shipping Company's Yongsheng ship, with a gross tonnage of 1,689 tons and a registered tonnage of 997 tons, set sail from Shanghai on the 9th of this month, loaded with groceries such as cloth and wood flour, for Quanzhou. On the 11th, it ran aground in Xiaozhuimen area on the coast of Quanzhou. The shipowner immediately telegraphed Shanghai to report. The company's office in Quanzhou sent a ship to rescue it and free it. After inspection, the damage to the bottom of the ship was very minor. It sailed to Quanzhou as usual, has already arrived, and started unloading. All passengers are safe. It has been decided to return to Shanghai after the cargo is unloaded.

China Merchants Bureau Reduces Expenditure Drastically 122

The China Merchants Bureau is quite large, and its expenses are also extremely high. Therefore, whenever business is slow, it feels the pain of not having enough income to cover expenses. After the reorganization this spring, in addition to making great efforts to develop business and increase income, the authorities also tried their best to reduce various expenditures. After the bureau publicly tendered for the various dock labors, it is expected to save more than 100,000 yuan per year, which has been published in the newspapers. According to reports, since February of this year, after the general bureau of the bureau screened and laid off employees, the number of staff in the departments has been reduced from 234 to 125, and the monthly salary has been reduced from more than 26,000 yuan to more than 16,000 yuan, saving an average of about 10,000 yuan per month. In addition, the bureau spent more than 230,000 yuan on ship repair costs from February to August of this year, which is approximately 110,000 yuan less than the 340,000 yuan spent in the same month last year. The materials and supplies used by ships and the maintenance costs of tugboats are much less than before. If it can continue to work hard to increase revenue and reduce expenditure, the future is immeasurable.

Jiangxi Guangda Porcelain Industry Company Capital Totaling 1 Million Yuan, Actively Prepared by Du Chongyuan 123

Jiangxi Guangda Porcelain Industry Co., Ltd. was initiated by Kong Yongzhi, Zhang Gongquan, Wu Tiecheng, Du Yuesheng, etc. It is being prepared by industrialist Du Chongyuan in Jiangxi. The headquarters and manufacturing plant will be established in Jiangxi. The capital amount is set at 1 million yuan in national currency, divided into 20,000 shares, each share is 50 yuan. The Jiangxi Provincial Government is recruiting in various places such as Hankou, Shanghai and Beijing, and has subscribed 200,000 yuan and guaranteed the payment of all dividends for the company for two years to promote and encourage. The first batch of large kilns costs 120,000 yuan, and the estimated cost for purchasing land, building factories and purchasing machinery is 1 million yuan. After the capital is fully received by the two banks of China and Xinhua in various places, construction will begin.

Shen Liren Establishes the Accounting System Research Association 124

The two types of income tax, namely, public servants' salaries and public bond interest, were levied from October 1st. Other parts will also start on New Year's Day next year. The time is short, but the levy of income tax on profitable enterprises and freelancers must rely on a precise accounting system as the standard. At the time when the new and old accounting systems are being replaced in our country, there are no prescribed standards for the names of accounts, the method of recording, and the calculation of depreciation and bad debts. If these problems are not resolved, it will be extremely difficult to collect income tax. Accountant Shen Liren has realized this, so he used his accounting system class taught at the School of Business of National Jinan University to organize an accounting system research association, with the students of the class as the basic members. The association is divided into four groups: one is the investigation group, specializing in investigating the characteristics of various industries and the old accounting system; one is the detailed research group, drafting accounting subjects applicable to various industries; one is the account design group, compiling the styles of account books and forms for various industries; and the fourth is the fraud prevention method research group, designing the organization of internal control to prevent fraud and increase work efficiency. At the same time, professors from the School of Business in the school are hired as review committee members to review the students' research results and publish them in journals for the reference of the industrial and commercial circles across the country. It will be of great help to the collection of income tax. Principal He and Dean Cheng Ruilin of the College of Commerce have greatly approved of the organization and have agreed to allocate funds for publishing and other expenses.

The board of directors of the British Shanghai Tram Company decided yesterday to pay a dividend of 4% for this year and set it to be issued on November 4.

More Than 500 Newly Arrived Japanese Sailors Paraded on North Sichuan Road Yesterday, Led by Officers Who Pointed Out the Direction of the Streets 126

According to the Central News Agency, the situation of the Japanese troops in North Sichuan Road and the urban area yesterday was more relaxed than the day before. There were still a small number of Japanese troops stationed in front of the Yongfeng Building on North Sichuan Road and the Japanese Elementary School, but there were no traces of Japanese troops at the remaining intersections. However, patrol teams and military vehicles still came and went from time to time and still crossed into the urban area. The number of Japanese troops in the Japanese distillery behind No. 63 Garden also decreased. However, around 5 PM yesterday, more than 500 newly arrived Japanese sailors, divided into about ten teams, were led by officers from the Marine Corps Headquarters, paraded along North Sichuan Road, Old Bazi Road, Zha Pu Road, and Haining Road, and stopped from time to time along the way. The officers gave instructions on the direction of the streets and the roads they lead to.

]Light and Bulky Goods: Revised Freight Calculation Method by the Ministry of Railways, Effective from the 1st 127

A report from the Central News Agency states: The Shanghai-Nanjing-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway Administration recently received an order from the Ministry of Railways stating that the current freight calculation method for light and bulky goods, stipulated in the Telex No. 3162, Ye Zi, dated May 31st of the 23rd year of the Republic (1934), has been convenient for full carloads of light and bulky goods since its implementation. However, for less-than-carload (LCL) shipments, the weight obtained from both measurement and weighing must be compared and then selected to calculate freight based on either the converted weight or the actual weight. This not only makes it difficult for merchants to know the amount of fees in advance but also makes the measurement procedures cumbersome. Furthermore, the volumes obtained from measurement by various railway lines often differ, adding difficulties to intermodal transport. The 9th National Railway Transportation Conference last year discussed the measurement system in detail and generally agreed that it needed improvement. Therefore, the Ministry has revised the freight calculation method for light and bulky goods, along with a list of special light and bulky goods and a list of ordinary light and bulky goods, which have been reviewed and approved by various railway lines. The revision of the light and bulky goods charging method does not significantly change the existing method for full carloads of light and bulky goods, as it is deemed quite suitable. However, for LCL shipments, the current measurement-based charging method will be abolished, and charges will be based on actual weight plus a surcharge, to simplify the process and benefit merchants. The newly revised freight calculation method for light and bulky goods is listed as follows:

(1) Goods with a weight of one kilogram and a volume exceeding three cubic decimeters but not exceeding four cubic decimeters are defined as ordinary light and bulky goods and listed in the "List of Ordinary Light and Bulky Goods." Goods with a weight of one kilogram and a volume exceeding four cubic decimeters are defined as special light and bulky goods and listed in the "List of Special Light and Bulky Goods."

(2) For full carloads of ordinary light and bulky goods, two-thirds of the car's carrying capacity is used as the minimum weight for calculating freight. For full carloads of special light and bulky goods, one-half of the car's weight is used as the minimum weight for calculating freight. If the actual weight exceeds the minimum weight, freight is calculated based on the actual weight. If open wagons are used for transportation, the loading height should at least be the same as that of covered wagons of the same tonnage, but it must not exceed the provisions of Article 79 of the Detailed Rules for the Transportation of Goods. When using covered wagons, the wagons must be fully loaded. If they are not fully loaded or do not reach the height of covered wagons of the same tonnage, freight should be calculated based on the car's weight.

(3) For LCL shipments of ordinary light and bulky goods, freight is calculated based on the actual total weight plus 20%. For LCL shipments of special light and bulky goods, freight is calculated based on the actual weight plus 50%.

All of the above three methods and the list of light and bulky goods will be implemented from October 1st of the 25th year of the Republic (1936). The current method will be abolished at the same time. Except for the relevant clauses of the General Rules for the Transportation of Goods, which will be revised separately, you are required to comply with and implement the above. After receiving the order, the railway line has implemented it from the 1st of this month. Our Newspaper Employee, Ge Guanfu, Murdered: Unhappy Family, Remarriage to a Loose Woman, Secret Affair with a Adulterer Leads to Brutal Attack 129

—Public Security Bureau Orders Strict Apprehension of the Murderer—

Ge Guanfu, an employee in the typesetting department of our newspaper, was suddenly attacked by his adulterous wife and her lover around 3:00 PM yesterday afternoon. They used a kitchen knife to sever his throat, killing him on the spot. When tenants upstairs heard the commotion, they rushed downstairs and alerted police officers on duty to give chase. However, both murderers managed to escape. The details are as follows:

Young but Prudent

Ge Guanfu, also known as Fu Chang, was a native of Wu County, Jiangsu Province. He was 35 years old and had been working as a typesetter in the typesetting department of our newspaper for nine years. He lived in a single-unit shikumen house at No. 11, Duoduo Lane, Daji Road, in the Nanshi district, acting as a second landlord. He lived in the living room downstairs, while the upstairs was rented out to others. Ge was naturally gentle and prudent, and he was known for his kindness and approachability. Throughout his service, he never had disagreements with his colleagues. Moreover, due to his diligence and dedication to his duties, his monthly income was sufficient for a modest living.

Portrait of the Deceased Ge Guanfu

Remarriage to a Loose Woman

Ge's late father passed away last year, and his stepmother lived with him. He had three sisters, two of whom were married, while one was still young. Ge's first wife, Zhang, passed away in January of the 22nd year of the Republic (1933), leaving behind a daughter named Gengdi, who is now seven years old. Four years ago, Ge remarried a woman from Wujin named Liu Xiangbao. She was 31 years old, fierce, and naturally promiscuous. It was rumored that she had a lover even before she married Ge. Ge, blinded by flattery, hastily remarried her, and soon after the marriage, domestic troubles arose, causing his colleagues to feel sorry for him.

Ousting the Stepmother and Cohabiting with a Lover

After marrying Ge, Liu bullied Ge's weakness and often turned against him. She would unleash her shrewish temper at the slightest dissatisfaction, but Ge always endured it without resistance. Little did he know that the seeds of murder were being sown. On the 20th of last month, Liu again displayed her shrewishness and abused Ge's stepmother. Terrified by her ferocity, Ge's mother immediately moved to No. 3, Linyin Road, nearby. Due to his duties at the newspaper, Ge had to go to work at the newspaper at 7:00 PM every night and could only return home after finishing work the next morning. Taking advantage of this opportunity, Liu, through the instigation of her younger brother Liu Zhisheng (who is currently an apprentice at Dada Cloth Shop at No. 11, Shengping Lane, Fada Avenue, and stopped working a week ago), began an affair with a man from Wujin named Lin Yakou, who worked at an eyewear store near the Old North Gate. They entered and exited Ge's home all day long and falsely claimed to Ge that they were cousins.

Accusation of Spousal Abuse

The adulterer, Lin, was a poorly dressed gigolo. He was in his thirties. Every night, when Ge went to work at the newspaper, Lin would become an intimate guest. Ge remained completely unaware. On the 6th of this month, Ge and Liu had another dispute over a minor matter. The next day, Liu went directly to Nanyang Hospital for a medical examination and filed a lawsuit against Ge for assault, demanding 30 yuan per month in alimony at the Shanghai Local Court. Ge also intended to file a counterclaim, and the summons had already been received and was scheduled to be heard at 2:00 PM today. However, neighbors were willing to testify truthfully for Ge. Little did they know that the tragedy would occur at 3:00 PM yesterday afternoon. On the morning of the 9th, Ge and his brother-in-law went to the hospital to persuade Liu to be discharged, but she refused.

Arriving at the Newspaper and Raising a Ruckus

On the evening of the 11th, at around 8:00 PM, Liu suddenly came to the newspaper to look for Ge. They then spent the night at the Asia Hotel on Sanma Road. The next day, Liu wanted to stay another night, but Ge, concerned about his work, firmly refused. They returned home together at 4:00 PM that afternoon. At around 7:00 PM, Ge intended to go to work at the newspaper, but Liu started to make a scene and refused to let Ge leave. Helpless, Ge stayed at home, causing him to be absent from work without leave, which was a violation of the rules. His colleagues were very worried, as they knew that Ge never neglected his work without a reason.

Sudden Murderous Attack

When Ge and Liu returned home from the Asia Hotel the day before yesterday, Ge's two sisters had been searching for them everywhere for a long time. When they saw their brother and sister-in-law returning, and noticed that Liu looked happy, they did not suspect anything and returned to their respective homes. At around 8:00 AM yesterday morning, Ge and Liu went out together and returned home at 3:00 PM, buying two new pairs of shoes. Little did they know that less than a quarter of an hour later, a tenant upstairs, Zhou Datong, was taking a nap when he suddenly heard a strange noise downstairs. He woke up in shock and rushed downstairs. However, there was no one downstairs. He entered Ge's bedroom and saw Ge lying in a pool of blood, wearing a white cloth shirt, trousers, white socks, and new shoes.

The Horrifying Scene of the Death

Ge was lying on the floor with his head resting on the side of the bed. Blood was gushing from his neck like a spring. The wound was about an inch deep and three inches long, and his throat was severed. He was barely breathing. The contents of the room were in disarray. At the same time, a kitchen knife was found near the door, covered in blood. Seeing this, Zhou rushed out to give chase. However, Liu was extremely cunning and, while fleeing in a panic, calmly carried a copper pot and hired a rickshaw to escape without a trace. The tenants reported the incident to the Ximen Branch of the Public Security Bureau, and Director Yao Guangnai immediately sent police officers to investigate.

Strict Apprehension of the Murderer

On the one hand, he instructed the local bailiff to report to the Shanghai Local Court to send personnel to conduct an autopsy. On the other hand, he ordered his subordinates to strictly apprehend the murderer and bring them to justice. At the same time, Ge's mother and two sisters rushed to the scene upon hearing the news and wept over the body. The colleagues of our newspaper also rushed to the scene one after another to inspect and express their deep condolences. The neighbors all sighed in distress. According to eyewitnesses, when Liu fled, she was seen carrying a copper pot and hastily hiring a rickshaw. When the police officers and neighbors chased after her, they saw the rickshaw she was in moving away quickly in front. However, at that time, many vehicles happened to pass by, blocking the view of the pursuers, causing Liu to disappear in an instant, which was truly regrettable. As to whether Ge Guanfu was murdered by the adulterous woman Liu Xiangbao alone or together with her lover Lin, it remains to be rigorously investigated when the murderer is apprehended.

Total Number of Automobiles in the Shanghai International Settlement Exceeds Ten Thousand 130

117 Types

According to the Shanghai Municipal Council Revenue Office, the number of motor vehicles in the Shanghai International Settlement that had been licensed by the end of September totaled 10,084. This includes 6,775 private cars, 420 taxis, 1,215 private trucks, 722 rental trucks, 170 public buses, 724 motorcycles, and 58 test vehicles. In terms of private cars, there are as many as 117 different types.

The Home Visit Campaign of the National Goods Promotion Association is Successful; The Women's National Goods Consumption Association is Scheduled to be Established This Month 131

Since the National Goods Promotion Association of this city launched its home visit campaign a dozen days ago, the work has been quite smooth. At the same time, the Women's National Goods Consumption Association organized by the association is also scheduled to be established this month. As for the national goods broadcasting, leaders in the national goods industry will continue to be invited to give lectures. The details are as follows:

Visiting Areas

The National Goods Promotion Association of this city, recognizing that women are the managers of the household and that their relationship with the promotion of national goods is very close, resolved to conduct home visits. To ensure seriousness, it also conducted strict examinations and selected Xu Chengqing, Xu Songzi, Chen Yingfen, Lin Wen, Shen Wenxian, etc. as visiting staff. The visiting staff had previously visited famous national goods factories in this city to study the production sequence of various national goods to provide a basis for implementing the visits. On September 25th, the visits officially began, starting from the Public Concession and the French Concession. The areas of Jing'an Temple Road, Yuyuan Road, Avenue Foch, Rue de Luynes, and Route de Ghisi have been completed. The second phase of visiting routes has been assigned as follows: Avenue Joffre (Shen Wenxian), Route Cardinal Mercier (Lin Wen), Route de Koukine (Chen Yingfen), Avenue Edward VII (Xu Songzi), Route Lafayette (Xu Chengqing).

Visiting Situation

Visiting staff depart on visits with badges and cards issued by the association to ensure formality, and they carry samples, gifts, and discount coupons from major national goods factories to distribute to housewives when inquiring or take out temporarily for identification. Since the visits began, the results have been quite good. Housewives in various families have warmly received the visiting staff and provided thoughtful comfort. They mostly approve of and are willing to use various national goods. If there are any dissatisfactions, they frankly express them and instruct the female visiting staff to inform the manufacturers to make improvements.

Scheduled Establishment

In order to promote the consumption of national goods by women, the association is preparing to form the Shanghai Women's National Goods Consumption Association. The wives of the association's committee members and the family members of managers and staff of various national goods factories have successively joined as members. Recently, when visiting staff made visits to various families, they also took the opportunity to persuade them. The housewives also recognized that consuming national goods is a duty that women should fulfill, and many filled out application forms on the spot and handed them over to the visiting staff to submit for membership. Therefore, even during the preparation period, the number of members has reached more than 500. It is heard that the association has scheduled its formal establishment this month.

National Goods Broadcasting

The association's national goods broadcasting lectures held every Tuesday afternoon from 5:20 to 5:40 PM on the Ministry of Communications Radio Station have been held thirteen times with great success. The association has now decided to continue until the end of this year. The list of continuing appointed speakers and dates is recorded below: Wang Jie'an, October 7th; Wang Hanqiang, October 27th; Zai Xingyi, November 3rd; Chen Yiting, November 10th; Jiang Xiaoqian, November 17th; Lu Lusha, November 24th; Li Aokui, December 1st; Zhong Zhaolin, December 8th; Chen Jiufeng, December 15th; Shao Daren, December 22nd; Gu Wensheng, December 29th.

Last Month's Factory Accidents in the Public Concession 133

Report from the Public Works Department's Factory Section: In September, 239 industrial and occupational accidents occurred in the Public Concession, resulting in the loss of 11 lives and injuries to 9 maids, two of whom did not survive. The causes of the accidents were generally clear in 216 cases, and investigations and measures for prevention and remediation were taken in 132 cases. Analyzing these dangerous incidents by industry type, 48 workers were injured in the machinery and metal manufacturing industry, but fortunately, there were no fatalities. Forty-six accidents occurred in the textile industry, resulting in 3 deaths. Forty-two accidents occurred in the transportation industry, resulting in 3 deaths. Twenty-eight accidents occurred in the building construction industry, resulting in 2 deaths. Five accidents occurred in the public utilities sector, resulting in 1 death. Seven accidents occurred in the chemical industry, resulting in 1 death. Analyzing the causes further, 79 dangerous incidents were related to electricity. Fourteen people were injured by axles and polishing machines, with 1 fatality. Sixteen people were injured by belts and gears, with no fatalities. Eleven people were injured by voltage machines, with no fatalities. Seven people were burned by fire, with 3 fatalities. Fifteen people were scalded by molten metal and corrosive substances. Forty people were injured from falling from heights, with 3 fatalities. Thirty-nine people were injured by falling objects, with no fatalities.

Accommodations and Meals Provided at the New Shanghai Inn

The Shanghai Zhejiang General Association has scheduled its 12th General Membership Meeting for the 18th. Your attendance is greatly anticipated. Sincerely, Shanghai Zhejiang General Association."

The Counterfeit Currency Operation Case on Wangzhi Road: Five Suspects to be Sentenced, Three Accused of No Prosecution: Taken to the Municipal Public Security Bureau for Interrogation 135

The Shanghai Municipal Public Security Bureau's Detective Team, last month, apprehended a suspect named Zhu Jinchang at the Yan Hai Lou teahouse in the Old North Gate, who confessed to manufacturing counterfeit banknotes of a certain bank in this city. He stated that the manufacturing operation was located inside No. 12 Dunrenfang, Wangzhi Road in the French Concession. Detectives, along with the suspect Zhu, reported to the French Police Station and dispatched detectives to the address, arresting the operation's owner, Chen Xinchang, and manufacturing workers Yu Kunshan, Liu Zhongde, Xiao Weibin, Zhu Lixing, and suspects Fan Shushan, Fan Wangshi, and Li Wangshi, a total of eight men and women. Two printing presses, a large quantity of counterfeit banknote paper blanks, 99 printed one-yuan counterfeit banknotes, and printing molds were seized. After investigation by the French Police Department, the five suspects Chen, Yu, Liu, Xiao, and Zhu were sent to the Special Second Court and prosecuted for counterfeiting currency. Fan Shushan, Fan Wangshi, and Li Wangshi were found to have no evidence of a crime and were not prosecuted. After interrogation by Judge Wang Gangxu, the Public Security Bureau sent personnel to the court, requesting the transfer of the case. Because the Police Department had already filed charges, they opposed the transfer. The court ordered a postponement of the interrogation. This matter has already been reported in this newspaper. Yesterday, Judge Wang continued the trial in Criminal Court No. 1. The Municipal Public Security Bureau again sent personnel to the court, requesting the transfer of the three suspects, Fan Shushan, Fan Wangshi, and Li Wangshi. After the court questioned the defendants one by one, they all confessed to privately manufacturing counterfeit currency. The court determined that the investigation and evidence were complete and ordered the opening of arguments. First, the Police Department's lawyer Gu Shouxi argued that the defendants had already confessed and should be severely punished according to law. For the defendants who were not prosecuted, he requested their release. After the defendants were defended by lawyer Zhu Dianqing, the court announced the conclusion of the arguments and scheduled the sentencing for the 20th. The five defendants, Chen, Yu, Liu, Xiao, and Zhu, were returned to custody. Fan Shushan, Fan Wangshi, and Li Wangshi were allowed to be taken by personnel from the Municipal Public Security Bureau for interrogation.

Another Passenger Jumps into the Sea from the Ningxing Steamer: A Shanghai Man Named Xu, Registration Clerk at a Hospital, Suicide Due to Heavy Family Burden and Economic Hardship 136

The Ningxing Steamer of the Sanbei Company, on a trip from Ningbo to Shanghai, had another passenger jump into the sea and commit suicide. Details are as follows:

Jumping into the Sea Late at Night

The Ningxing Steamer was sailing from Shanghai to Ningbo. In Cabin No. 25, there was a middle-aged passenger who was also traveling to Ningbo on the steamer. It was decided that when the steamer arrived in Ningbo in the morning, the passenger did not disembark, claiming to have forgotten belongings in Shanghai and needed to return to Shanghai to retrieve them. Therefore, the steamer sailed from Ningbo to Shanghai the following afternoon, and the passenger still took the same cabin back to Shanghai. Unexpectedly, around 11 PM that night, the tea server Dai Alian noticed that the cabin door was ajar. Upon entering to check, the passenger was nowhere to be found.

Details of the Deceased

The tea server then inspected the passenger's berth and discovered a package of belongings and a letter. The envelope was addressed to the Shanghai Charity Hospital at No. 97 North Chengdu Road, Shanghai, with a request to the tea server to deliver it on their behalf. It was then realized that the passenger had committed suicide by jumping into the sea. The steamer returned to Shanghai yesterday, and the tea server delivered the belongings and letter to the address. It was learned that the deceased was a Shanghai native named Xu, a registration clerk at the Charity Hospital. The cause of suicide was said to be due to an excessive family burden and economic hardship.

Shanghai Postal Administration Notice No. 2362 states: "Regarding the flight schedule for the China National Aviation Corporation's Chongqing-Guiyang route, which was previously announced by this Bureau in Public Notice No. 13054, we have now received a letter from the company stating that flights on the Chongqing-Guiyang route are originally scheduled to fly back and forth twice a week on Tuesdays and Saturdays. However, as it is now autumn and daylight hours are shorter, the flight from Chongqing to Guiyang, originally scheduled for 2:00 PM, is now changed to 12:00 PM. The flight from Guiyang to Chongqing, originally scheduled for 3:15 PM, is now changed to 2:15 PM. All flight times for this route will be advanced by one hour, effective September 26th (Saturday) of this year. Please take note." Approved. This notice is hereby issued for public awareness. Director Zha Peilin, October 19th.

YWCA Labor Department's Double Tenth Festival Commemoration 138

The YWCA Labor Department, in order to promote female workers' sense of unity, initiative, and spirit of cooperation, held an autumn gathering for workers from the 2nd to the 4th of this month at the Ye Family Ancestral Hall in Meilong. Forty-three representatives from the Yangshupu, Gongping Road, Pudong, Labosan Road, Caishi Road, and Tilanqiao school worker groups participated (representing the association's four schools, two women's association schools, and 788 workers). The order of the meeting was planned and presided over by the workers themselves. Detailed speeches, debates, and discussions were held on issues of national crisis, improving workers' lives, and worker leadership. All participants deeply felt the great mission that female workers should undertake in the future. On the 11th of this month, a Double Tenth Festival commemoration was held at the association's location, with over 300 participants. At 2:00 PM, the chair announced the opening of the meeting, followed by the opening ceremony, and explained the reason for holding the commemoration on the day after the Double Tenth Festival. The entire group sang "The Chinese Nation Will Not Perish." Ms. Jiang Ping gave a speech on "The Significance of Commemorating the Double Tenth Festival." Following this, the school worker groups took turns presenting programs. The Yangshupu workers performed the opera "The Masters of China." The Gongping Road worker representatives gave a speech on "How to Commemorate the Double Tenth Festival." The Labosan Road workers performed the mime "Recover Our Territory." The Pudong workers performed the tragedy "The Abandoned Child." The Caishi Road workers performed the new play "The Workers' Home." The atmosphere was very solemn, especially during the final play, which moved the audience to tears of grief and indignation. Fortunately, the meeting concluded with a majestic song from the entire group, and the participants left with a sense of responsibility and joy.

Longjiang Pier Dock Worker Falls and Drowns 139

Shen Genfa, a 29-year-old Shanghai native and night watchman for the Chuangxin Construction Factory, which is building the Bund Longjiang Pier in the city center, was assisting in pushing wooden rafts outside the pier in the river around 5:00 PM on the 9th of this month. Due to his unfamiliarity with water activities, he lost his footing and fell into the river, tragically drowning. His body floated to the surface near the scene of the incident at 10:00 AM yesterday. It was recovered by the Customs Water Patrol Police. Detective Liang Qing notified the deceased's sister, Xu Shenshi, and requested the local court to send personnel for examination.

Page 12

The Hongkou Women's Hospital Corpse Burial Case: Sentencing Scheduled, Witnesses Summoned to Testify Yesterday, Zhang Wenhua Changes Testimony, Claiming It Was Due to Surgical Carelessness 140

—Prosecutor Argues for Severe Punishment—

Zhang Wenhua, a 27-year-old Shanghai native and doctor at the Hongkou Women's Hospital at No. 290 Zhaofeng Road, and his concubine assistant nurse Chen Xiaobao (also known as Liang Meiyu and Xu Shuzhen, 25 years old, Shanghai native) were arrested and sent to the First Special Court for allegedly killing a woman from Sichuan named Lu Aili and a man named Yu Gengsheng on September 4th of this year and burying their bodies underground. The case was discovered by Chinese Detective Zhou Guisen and Detectives Cui Chengke and Huang Fugeng of the Huishan Police Station, who arrested Zhang Wenhua and Chen Xiaobao at No. 13, Lane 455, Tiyuan Road, French Concession, on the 2nd of this month. The police station filed charges of murder according to Article 271 of the Criminal Law. After the Special Court's initial interrogation, both defendants admitted that Zhang Wenhua had performed an abortion on Lu Aili, but due to anger, the surgery was rough, causing the uterus to rupture, resulting in unstoppable bleeding and a critical condition. At the same time, Yu Gengsheng negotiated with Zhang, leading to a murderous intent. Zhang injected Yu with an anesthetic needle and strangled both the man and woman with gauze. The court ordered further interrogation after summoning witnesses, as previously reported in this newspaper. Yesterday morning, Judge Zhong Qing and Prosecutor Zhang Zongru continued the trial in Criminal Court No. 3.

The number of men and women in the audience was still very crowded. Both defendants hired lawyers Fan Gang and Yu Enliang to defend them. The police station's lawyer Zhang Shizhu stated that all the witnesses summoned by the court, except for the maid Fei Wangshi who had returned to Wuxi, had arrived in court. He requested to question them. The witness Chen Pengfei testified that he was 23 years old, a Shanghai native, and lived at No. 704 Renzhi Lane, North Sichuan Road. The defendant Chen Xiaobao was his sister, and Zhang Wenhua was his employer. He worked for Zhang as a driver from August 29th of this year. Zhang's original name was Lao Wang, so he usually

called him Lao Wang. The Hongkou Women's Hospital was opened by the two defendants. The witness Yang Yufu testified that he was a night watchman at the church at No. 188 Zhaofeng Road. The remaining rooms of the Hongkou Hospital were rented by Zhang Wenhua. Chen Xiaobao was Zhang's concubine. Ren Lijin, the manager of the Huiyuanxiang Hardware Store at No. 203 Tangshan Road, testified that Chen Xiaobao came to his store early in the morning on September 4th to purchase six sheets of lead, totaling five yuan and three jiao. Tan Xiquan, a clerk at the Taifei Lime Store at No. 89 Xinji Hong Road, testified that on the morning of September 4th, Chen Xiaobao came with an eleven or twelve-year-old girl to

purchase 150 pounds of lime, totaling one yuan and four jiao. Chen Linchang, a carpenter at the Chen Linji Carpentry Shop at No. 314 Zhaofeng Road, testified that the Hongkou Women's Hospital was diagonally across from his shop, so he knew Zhang Wenhua. One morning, Zhang came to borrow an iron bar, saying he needed it to pry open a wooden board. He lent it to him, and it was returned the next morning. When questioned, Zhang Wenhua and the others did not object to the witnesses' statements. However, they claimed that the more than 900 yuan in cash seized was accumulated savings and was deposited in the bank. After the incident, they withdrew

more than 300 yuan from the Zhejiang Industrial Bank and more than 100 yuan from the Jincheng Bank, totaling 450 yuan, for living expenses. The male and female victims were confirmed to be from Sichuan, but their origin was not disclosed because the abortion was a secret. The female corpse had 40 yuan on her, of which 35 yuan was paid for the abortion, leaving 5 yuan. Therefore, it was not a case of murder for money. This point can be investigated. After burying the bodies, they moved to No. 6 Min Village, Mintiniyin Road, on September 7th, because Zhang's clinic, in addition to the Hongkou Hospital, was also located at Room 315, 3rd Floor, Dalu Commercial Building, Nanjing Road,

rented from Dr. Hou Guangdi for 20 yuan a month, specializing in treating common illnesses. Another clinic was established at No. 370 Balibridge Road in the French Concession. Therefore, from the time of the incident until before the case was discovered, he continued to provide consultations at Balibridge Road. On September 10th, a woman came for an abortion and paid a fee of 50 yuan. He requested that all the wooden objects seized by the police at his location be sent to his father, Zhang Jinsheng, at No. 39 Weide Lane, Guangdong Street, Gaochang Temple, Nanshi. At this time, the police station's lawyer Zhang Shizhu stated that although the two defendants had confessed during the previous trial that they had

killed Yu and Lu with anesthetic needles and then strangled them with gauze, according to the forensic report, the two victims were indeed strangled to death. Therefore, it should be determined whether they were strangled to death or strangled after death. Judge Zhong then questioned Zhang Wenhua. Unexpectedly, Zhang suddenly changed his testimony, claiming that the woman Lu Aili had indeed suffered a uterine rupture during the abortion due to his carelessness, causing blood to enter her abdomen, leading to anemia, unconsciousness, and a critical condition. At that time, Yu Gengsheng was ringing the bell downstairs. He went downstairs and

negotiated with him greatly. He thought that in order to remedy the situation, he needed to draw blood and infuse it into the woman's body. So, he went upstairs to draw blood with a needle. Unexpectedly, he carelessly sucked air into Yu's blood vessels while drawing blood, causing Yu to die. When he went downstairs, he saw that Lu had also died. To prevent odor and fluid from escaping, he wrapped gauze around their necks, but he did not strangle them to death. If there had been strangulation at the time, Yu and the others would have naturally resisted, and the night watchman Yang Yufu, who was sleeping in the next room, would have heard something. Therefore, the deaths of the two were due to momentary carelessness,

not intentional murder. His statements today were all true and without any falsehood. The previous statements were made in a confused state due to being frightened during the arrest. Chen Xiaobao also stated that Lu Aili died from the abortion, and Yu Gengsheng died from drawing blood. She had practiced nursing at the Guangci Hospital on Jin Shenfu Road for three months and had been living with Zhang for more than two years. The court verified the statements and determined that the facts of the case were clear. The court ordered the start of arguments. First, the police station's lawyer Zhang Shizhu stated that the two defendants specialized in performing abortions as a regular business and that this type of behavior

involved harming people without any resistance and was extremely vicious. He requested that they be sentenced to the most severe punishment. Finally, the defendants' lawyers Fan Gang and Yu Enliang argued that, according to the circumstances of the previous trials, the two defendants did not intentionally commit murder. This case originated from an abortion, and they should be sentenced according to the crime of abortion due to professional negligence. Chen Xiaobao was also pregnant and requested that her sentence be executed after she gave birth.

Prosecutor Zhang's concluding remarks stated that, according to the circumstances of this case, it was not like an ordinary murder case. The defendants not only killed people with slippery medical skills and treated human lives as a game, but their actions were also like bandits running a black shop. After the murder, they destroyed the corpses and eliminated the evidence, which was extremely vicious. If they were not severely punished, it would be insufficient to maintain public morality and the protection of the law. Judge Zhong ordered the conclusion of arguments and scheduled the sentencing for the morning of the 20th of this month. Both defendants were returned to custody separately.

New Traffic Regulations for the Public Concession to Take Effect Tomorrow 141

Yesterday, the Public Concession's Municipal Council issued Notice No. 4714 (regarding the amendment of traffic regulations), stating: Notice is hereby given that Articles 1, 28, 47, and 48 of the traffic regulations have been approved for amendment as follows and will take effect from October 15, 1936. The amendments to Article 1 involve deleting the definitions of "straight parking vehicles" and "parallel parking vehicles" and replacing them with the following two definitions: Long-term parking: refers to vehicles parked on the street for a considerable period. Short-term parking: refers to vehicles parked on streets outside approved parking locations, with time restrictions. Article 28 has been amended as follows: Article 28. Drivers shall not temporarily park vehicles or stop at any location on the street (except when complying with signals given by traffic police) (A) where "No Parking" signs are erected, or the roadside stones are painted red, or with black and white tiles; (B) parallel to tram stops; (C) within 30 feet of any major thoroughfare corner; (D) between traffic islands and roadside stones. Article 47 has been amended as follows: Article 47. Vehicles are not allowed to "long-term park" on the street, except at approved locations, but short-term parking is permitted within reasonable limits and time. Ticket Collector Jumps to His Death 142

A ticket collector named Yang from the Sun Sun Company jumped from the sixth floor at 1:35 this morning, dying instantly. The body was sent to Renji Hospital for examination.

Monk Bingnan Accused of Assault Again 143

Bingnan, a monk from Zhenjiang and the abbot of Zhulin Temple at 109 Longmen Road, aged 61, was previously sued in the First Special District Court by his widowed sister-in-law, Yuan Ge, for raping her and her daughter-in-law, Zhao Cuizhen. After a special trial, Bingnan was found not guilty. The court's judgment was appealed to the Second Branch of the High Court, but the appeal was rejected. Now, Yuan Ge has hired lawyer Huang Xiubo to file an assault lawsuit against Bingnan in the First Special District Court. The facts are that on October 3, the plaintiff went to the defendant's residence to retrieve clothing. Unexpectedly, the defendant used a wooden clothes-beating stick to strike the plaintiff's right ribs, left arm, right waist, and head, causing bruises all over the body. The plaintiff cried out, and Chinese constable No. 3026 arrived before the defendant released her. Subsequently, the Chengdu Road police station was notified and sent detectives to arrest the defendant and take him to the police station. The plaintiff was sent to Renji Hospital for treatment. The chief constable instructed the plaintiff to file a lawsuit in court, so she went to the prosecutor's office of the First Special District Court to have her injuries examined and then filed a lawsuit, requesting punishment under Article 277, Paragraph 1 of the Criminal Law. Yesterday afternoon, Judge Zhan Liangce opened the Ninth Criminal Court to hear the case, and Chinese constable No. 3026 was also summoned to testify. Bingnan claimed that Yuan Ge attacked him first, slapping him in the face. After the court verified the statements, it adjourned the hearing to a later date.

Counterfeit Coin Operation Busted on Connaught Road; Mastermind at Large, Two Accomplices Arrested 144

Xu Zhengting, a Chinese detective from the Sinza Police Station, recently discovered that someone was secretly manufacturing Central Bank one-dollar counterfeit coins for profit at No. 30, Lane 580, Connaught Road. He applied to the First Special District Court for Search Warrant No. 233. The previous morning at 11:00 AM, he and a Western detective went to No. 30 and arrested Song Qing, a native of Shaoxing, without raising suspicion. No evidence was found. However, the house had a partition connecting to No. 32. They entered and found the counterfeit coin manufacturing operation. Yang Jiazhen, a native of Pinghu, and Sun Baohua, a native of Wuxi, were unable to escape and were arrested. They were taken to the police station along with three manufacturing machines, two wooden molds, one small printing machine, and a large bundle of banknote paper. Yesterday morning, Wang Yaotang, a lawyer from the Public Works Department, filed a public prosecution in the Eighth Criminal Court under Article 199 of the Criminal Law for counterfeiting currency. He stated that the mastermind was Wang Amao, who was at large, and the three defendants were hired accomplices. He requested a postponement, and the three large printing machines were temporarily stored at the police station because it was inconvenient to bring them to court. Subsequently, Detective Xu reported the details of the bust, and the small machines and paper were presented for inspection. When questioned, Sun Baohua confessed that Wang Amao had invited him to work at the operation during the Mid-Autumn Festival. The banknotes had not yet been printed, and Wang Amao had purchased the machines. He pleaded for leniency. The two defendants, Yang and Song, claimed that they had recently received a letter from their friend Tang Qianming from their hometown, introducing them to the operation to help out. Their other statements were evasive. Judge Huang Risheng ordered them to be remanded in custody and rescheduled the hearing for seven days later.

The Women and Children's Welfare Home to Hold its 15th Anniversary 146

The Shanghai Women and Children's Welfare Home on Xiangyin Road in Jiangwan, founded by the Chinese Women's Temperance Association, is the pioneer of Chinese women-run charitable organizations. Its purpose is to rescue women and children beggars, maids, abandoned women, and other unfortunate women. Its economic sources, in addition to a portion of the institution's production, are subsidies from the competent authorities of the membership fees collected from members. When this is insufficient, it solicits donations from the outside world. Over the past fifteen years, thanks to the efforts of the administrators and the support of the outside world, no less than several thousand women and children have benefited from it. This autumn, the Temperance Association plans to celebrate the past and encourage the future by holding its 15th anniversary this month. Mao Kelun, Wu Chengyu, Li Zhongdao, and their wives have been publicly elected to prepare everything.

Counterfeit Coin Operation Case at Xiaodongmen; Local Court Hearing; Defendants Consistently Deny Guilt; Result to be Announced After Investigation and Further Hearing 148

Chen Yunsheng, a native of Shaoxing, and Cheng Guanglu and Liu Jinshuan, who are at large, jointly established a counterfeit currency operation at No. 46, Lujiazhai, Xiaodongmen, manufacturing counterfeit Central Bank banknotes. Zhou Yongtian, Liu Qinghua, and Zhuang Hongfu were assigned to transport and perform various other tasks. Tianjin, Yancheng, and other places were their largest sales outlets. This was discovered by the Nanjing Branch of the Shanghai Public Security Bureau, which sent police to search the premises on the 26th of last month. They seized 1,000 yuan in Central Bank counterfeit banknotes, copper plates, chemicals, and other items. Chen Yunsheng, Zhou Yongtian, Liu Qinghua, and Zhuang Hongfu were arrested on the spot, while Cheng and Liu escaped. The Public Security Bureau transferred the suspects and evidence to the local court's prosecutor's office. Prosecutor Lei Binzhang filed a public prosecution, stating that Chen Yunsheng, Cheng Guanglu, and Liu Jinshuan had counterfeited Central Bank banknotes, as Chen Yunsheng had confessed, and the seized counterfeit banknotes and copper plates were proof. Zhuang Hongfu admitted to cooking for Chen and knowing that he was counterfeiting banknotes. Liu Qinghua admitted to transporting counterfeit banknotes. It was clear that they were jointly counterfeiting and sharing work. Zhou Yongtian cunningly denied it, but he was arrested at the counterfeit currency operation and claimed that he had just arrived in Shanghai from Yantai and was staying at Chen's residence. He also claimed that a girl was being fostered there, but he did not know her name. When questioned, Chen Yunsheng claimed that the girl was his niece, and her mother's family name was Wang. Zhou Yongtian claimed that the girl did not live there. It was clear that Zhou Yongtian and Chen Yunsheng were accomplices in the case, so they lived in the same room. Otherwise, how could others live in a place that was a counterfeit currency operation? The defendants' actions constituted a crime under Article 28 and Article 195, Paragraph 1 of the Criminal Law. The prosecution was filed in accordance with Article 230, Paragraphs 1 and 2 of the Criminal Procedure Law. He requested the court to punish them according to law. Yesterday, Judge Miao opened the court for a hearing. The defendants hired lawyer Xu Heling to defend them. Because they all denied their guilt, the court ordered that the case be investigated further and reheard.

Maritime Customs Restricts Towboats Alongside Ships 161

The Jianghai Customs Port Affairs Department, in order to maintain traffic on the Huangpu River, issued a proclamation restricting the number of barges alongside ships. The original text reads: "According to Article 45 of the Shanghai Port Management Regulations for Ships, the circumstances and number of barges and civilian boats alongside large ships must not obstruct the navigation of other ships in the port. In order to allow other barges and ships to have free passage in the port, the number of ships alongside each row shall be limited as follows: (1) Iron barges with a capacity of 100 tons or more are limited to two ships side by side per row. (2) Iron barges with a capacity of less than 100 tons are limited to three ships side by side per row. Note: This regulation only applies to iron barges whose capacity tonnage is clearly marked in large letters on both sides of the hull or superstructure. (3) Chinese barges are limited to six ships side by side per row. No other ships are allowed to moor outside the ships specified above. Any ships violating the regulations of this chapter will be immediately fined by this department. Merchants are hereby notified."

Shenbao National Goods Special Issue

"Eliminating Import Surplus" and "Frugality Movement" 171

— Xuan Wan

Everyone knows that our country's huge import surplus in recent years is the fatal injury that has led to the bankruptcy of our national economy. At present, when our country's economic crisis is so serious, we must "eliminate the import surplus" and "promote frugality," which is the only way to save the national economic crisis. In the entire national economic construction movement, we must develop national products to eliminate the import surplus and implement frugality to increase national power. These are the basic conditions for enriching the country and strengthening the people.

However, in the past, the huge annual import surplus included many imported luxury goods, such as perfume, cosmetics, genuine and fake jewelry, cigarettes, cigars, various alcoholic beverages, soda, candy, shark fin, bird's nest, and the like. These many expensive things should not be consumed in such large quantities today when the people are poor and resources are exhausted, but facts speak louder than words. In the recent - September 30th Shenbao, we still saw that in the first eight months of this year, the import of tobacco and alcohol alone reached more than 12 million yuan, and the import of cigarettes has increased significantly compared to last year. I think no one will be satisfied with this and feel that the future of the national goods movement still requires greater efforts!

Therefore, in the same day's newspaper, we also saw the "Frugality Movement" speech delivered by Minister Wu of the Ministry of Industry on the 29th of this month at the Central Broadcasting Station in the capital. I think it is very agreeable. He succinctly and clearly pointed out that China's annual consumption of clothing, food, housing, and articles reaches 360 million yuan. This alone is enough to show the crisis of the Chinese economy. From now on, we must all save materials to accumulate national power. The more materials we save, the more we increase national power. He also explained that if everyone can save one yuan per year, the vitality of the national economy can be increased by 400 million yuan throughout the year. These many words are very poignant, earnest, and worth our every person's deep reflection.

Finally, with fervent hope, I want the current "Frugality Movement" to start with refusing to use imported luxury goods and be linked with the entire national goods promotion movement. We must all recognize the difficult times, make a firm decision, save and spend carefully, and work hard on production and construction to "reduce the import surplus" and even completely "eliminate the import surplus," opening a new path for the future of national goods. This is the fundamental plan to save the country and ourselves!

Contribution Talk

Thinking of Mr. Xiang Songmao from the 30th Anniversary of Wuzhou 172

— Yang An

Like mustard seeds, regard money as gold,

Like the public, together forge gold,

The cause of Baling for thirty years,

The medicine records a lifetime's heart.

Diligently plug the leakage of the zhi,

Thinking about rising and falling,

This is truly not cracking the hand,

Difficult tasks can be undertaken.

In the middle of the night, the sound of war rises,

Orioles and flowers are sadly not spring,

With hat and crown, step on the tiger's tail,

Resisting the rhythm, offending the dragon's scales,

Already achieved the will to become benevolent,

Difficult to forget the hardship of starting a business.

Report respect and leave eternal thoughts,

Loyalty and courage are always new in history.

This is the poem written by the author for the completion of Songmao Memorial Hall. As we celebrate the 30th anniversary of Wuzhou, and the completion of the new ten-story building, it is most meaningful and valuable to commemorate the martyrdom of Mr. Songmao. Mr. Songmao left a patriotic spirit to the country and society, which is unparalleled in its greatness and will never be erased. Mr. Huang Renzhi said that "the foundation of Wuzhou's ten-story building is built on Mr. Songmao's loyalty and courage, that is, on the spirit of loyalty, courage, and martyrdom." Mr. Wang Xiaolai said, "Today, tens of thousands of people come here, admiring not the ten-story building, nor envying the 30-year great career, but attracted by Mr. Songmao's spirit of sacrificing his career and his country." All of these are valuable words. Mr. Songmao engaged in the national goods business for thirty years, with extraordinary nature, meticulous, and regarded the people in the company as family members and disciples. Upon hearing that someone in the company was arrested, he immediately went to rescue them, and his spirit of regarding death as home and not avoiding danger can inspire future generations. The development and growth of Wuzhou's business to today's achievements can be said to be the crystallization of Mr. Songmao's efforts, and can also be said to be filled with Mr. Songmao's will and courage. Mr. Songmao has always had self-encouraging words of thirty characters, which can be recited and will never be extinguished. The sentence says:

In ordinary times, one should reduce desires to nurture the body,

When facing great events, one should accept fate and entrust life.

When managing a family, one must live within one's means,

When pursuing great righteousness, one should regard money as mustard seeds.

These thirty characters can show the personality of Mr. Songmao, and the development and prosperity of Wuzhou's business is indeed without end. What is desired is that those in charge take Mr. Songmao's will as their own, take Mr. Songmao's heart as their own, and take Mr. Songmao's way of treating people and dealing with the world as their rule, then Mr. Songmao will not die but live on. Not only that, but in the future, Wuzhou's business should improve its products to surpass imported goods, reduce costs to benefit patients, and research Chinese medicine to improve it and integrate Chinese and Western medicine into one furnace to enhance its effectiveness. These are all Mr. Songmao's unfinished ambitions, which are waiting for today's authorities to complete. If this can be done, it will not only be the luck of Wuzhou, the glory of the national goods industry, but also the glory of the Republic of China.

Tianxu Wosheng Invents Method of Manufacturing Wood Pulp from Match Waste 173

— Qingbo

There is more than one Chinese match stick factory, and more than one type of wood is used, but all use planing, and the outer layer of the Zheng and the inner core of the remaining wooden sticks have always been used as fuel, which is a pity. In the 21st year of the Republic of China, Chen Diexian (alias Tianxu Wosheng), the founder of the paper mill, specially consulted with Feng Xizhi, the manager of the Guanghua Match Factory in Zhejiang Province, to request that the aforementioned waste materials be supplied for the factory's papermaking, and paper samples were made and sent to Mr. Feng, one for bleached material and one for natural color material, both of which can be used as wood pulp substitutes. However, due to the high moisture content, the obtained composition is only 13 to 15 percent, and the cost of transportation from Hangzhou to Tin is not cost-effective, so it was not implemented. Now that Chen Diexian has been hired by the Zhejiang Provincial Construction Department as a special commissioner for improving paper material design, he is starting to build stoves and ponds in Fancun. In addition to using bamboo material and wild hemp bark, he is also considering using match waste materials, which can be obtained nearby. Therefore, he entrusted Mr. Feng Xizhi to re-propose the old proposal. The price and monthly quantity were agreed upon on the 25th of this month at Jiangzhuang, Dingxiang Bridge in West Lake, and all were contracted and consumed by the provincial-run improved paper material factory. Chen Diexian also agreed to publicly teach the manufacturing method so that colleagues in the match factory industry in various places can locally produce wood pulp and purchase tree bark stripped from firewood shops and this industry to supplement the composition. The wood used for charcoal burning in various places can also have its bark removed first to produce wood pulp for sale to various paper factories.

Messrs. Junmei, Yao Mingran, Qiao Yunxun, and Qiuying, please supplement your seals and send a letter in your own handwriting for verification and issuance.
